1935.02.22

Chiang Kai-shek Arrives in Hankou by Ship

Meets with Zhang Xueliang, He Chengjun, and Others

Inspects Hankou Municipal Administration by Car

[Hankou] Chairman Chiang departed Nanchang at noon on the 20th and transferred to the Yong Sui warship at Xunyang at 10:00 PM, with the Xianning warship escorting. Yang Yongtai, Yan Xunfu, Yan Daogang, Mao Qingxiang, Wang Rizhang, and others accompanied him. Arrived in Hankou at 2:30 PM on the afternoon of the 21st. Zhang Xueliang, He Chengjun, Zhang Qun, Qian Dajun, Ye Peng and other important military and political figures welcomed him at Sanbei Wharf. Chiang, in military uniform, disembarked with his wife, Soong Mei-ling, and proceeded to the Central Bank office. He summoned Zhang Xueliang, He Chengjun, and Zhang Qun, inquiring about the bandit suppression military affairs and political arrangements. He instructed the remaining personnel to return to their posts and work as usual, awaiting further summons. (Special dispatch from the 21st)

[Hankou] After meeting with Zhang Xueliang, He Chengjun, and Zhang Qun, Chairman Chiang then met with Qian Dajun and others. That evening, he and his wife inspected the Hankou municipal administration by car for about an hour before returning to the office. It was decided that he would summon the provincial and municipal party committees on the 22nd to inquire about party affairs. Yang Yongtai and Zhang Qun went to Wuchang to stay overnight on the evening of the 21st. (Special dispatch from the 21st)

[Hankou] The Wuchang Headquarters is scheduled to be established on March 1st, with Zhang Xueliang as the director. The remaining senior personnel will be announced by Chiang's order within the next few days. (Special dispatch from the 21st)

[Hankou] Chen Jicheng arrived in Hankou on the 21st to await an audience with Chiang. Xu Yuanquan will also fly to Hankou to report on military affairs to Chiang and request instructions. (Special dispatch from the 21st)

[Hankou] The Transportation Office of the Jiangxi Headquarters moved to Hubei in compliance with orders. All personnel, led by Director Lin Xiang, arrived in Hankou and are now working inside the Wuchang Mint. (Special dispatch from the 21st)

[Hankou] Chairman Chiang and his wife arrived in Hankou at 3:00 PM on the afternoon of the 21st aboard the Yong Sui warship, accompanied by Secretary-General Yang Yongtai. They docked at Sanbei Wharf. Zhang Xueliang, He Chengjun, Zhang Qun, Chen Xizeng, Ye Peng, Zhang Zhen, and others were waiting on the shore. Chiang, in military uniform and wearing a black wool cloak, looked radiant. As he disembarked, he smiled and greeted the welcomers. He then boarded a car to the Central Bank residence for rest. Zhang Xueliang and others went to pay their respects. (Central News Agency dispatch from the 21st)

[Hankou] Chairman Chiang of the Military Affairs Commission went to Jiangxi a week ago to handle military affairs. Having now completed his duties, and with the Wuchang Headquarters decided to be officially established on March 1st, he departed Nanchang on the 20th to come to Hankou. He originally planned to fly to Hankou at noon on that day, but upon receiving a telegram from Hankou stating that the weather in Wuhan was unfavorable and there was heavy rain, making it inconvenient to fly, he temporarily changed his plans and departed Nanchang by special train to Xunyang at 3:00 PM on the afternoon of the 20th. That evening, he transferred to the Yong Sui warship to travel west, with the Xianning warship carrying important staff from the Nanchang Headquarters following behind to provide escort. Both warships arrived safely in Hankou at 3:00 PM on the afternoon of the 21st. Upon receiving news that the Yong Sui warship had left Xunyang and was heading west, all circles in Wuhan went to Sanbei Wharf on the afternoon of the 21st to welcome him, with Zhang Xueliang, He Chengjun, Zhang Qun, and others numbering no less than a thousand people. Security at the Sanbei Company Wharf was provided by the Minsheng warship, the Navy, the 1st Regiment of the Central Military Police, the Garrison Brigade, the Special Service Battalion, and police officers from the Public Security Bureau. The river surface was patrolled and maintained by patrol boats dispatched by the Water Police Bureau. At that time, the rain had stopped and the sky had cleared, and the road was free of dust, making the order seem even more solemn and neat. At 3:00 PM, the Yong Sui and Xianning warships arrived. Welcoming personnel lined up and waited on the lighter. Before long, the Yong Sui warship docked, and Chairman Chiang and his wife, Madame Soong Mei-ling, disembarked amidst the navy playing music and firing cannons. The welcoming personnel stood in solemn respect. Chiang, dressed in military uniform and wearing a black wool cloak, looked radiant and nodded his head in thanks. As he disembarked, the military band of the Garrison Department played music to welcome him, and the military police stood at attention to pay their respects. Chiang then boarded a car with Deputy Commander Zhang to rest at the Central Bank residence. Madame Chiang was accompanied by Deputy Commander Zhang's wife, Yu Fengzhi, and Chairman Zhang's wife, and took another car ahead. After Chiang arrived at the Central Bank, he met with Director He, Chairman Zhang, and others, and inquired about the military and political situation in Hubei Province. He and Zhang then excused themselves. As for the remaining party, government, and military personnel, they will be summoned at a later date. Those who came to Hankou with Chiang included Secretary-General Yang Yongtai, Director Yan Xunfu, and Yan Daogang, Mao Qingxiang, Wang Rizhang, Chen Fang, and others. The remaining staff below the rank of section chief at the Nanchang Headquarters arrived in Hankou on the Jiangxin liner at 8:00 PM on the 21st. A Central News Agency reporter visited Secretary-General Yang and Director He, and heard Director He say that Secretary-General Yang had gone to Wuchang to handle official business, and that the Chairman's visit to Hankou would be a long one. (Central News Agency dispatch from the 21st)

Central Standing Committee Passes Proposals on Etiquette Systems

[Nanjing] The Central Committee held its 159th Standing Committee meeting at 8:00 AM on the 21st. More than twenty people attended, including Wang Zhaoming, Ju Zheng, Ye Chucang, Sun Ke, Lin Sen, Shao Yuanchong, Chu Minyi, Chen Lifu, Ma Chaojun, and Li Zonghuang. Wang Zhaoming chaired the meeting and discussed several proposals. Regarding Chairman Chiang Kai-shek's suggestions on the etiquette system, after detailed discussion, the following resolutions were made: (1) Regarding the manufacture and use of the Party and National flag, in addition to the existing regulations on the manufacture and use of the Party and National flag, the management of manufacturing and selling stores should be supplemented according to Article 2 of the original regulations. (2) The various provisions of the regulations on the manufacture and use of the Party and National flag should be earnestly enforced by the Capital Police Department, the Civil Affairs Departments of the provinces, and the Municipal Governments of the cities. (3) The rectification of ceremonial attire for holding ceremonies was generally approved, and the Standing Committee will appoint personnel to review the measures. (4) Regarding the prohibition of newspapers directly addressing the name of the Chairman of the National Government, it was handed over to the Propaganda Committee for implementation. Also, Commissioner Mu Song was designated to give a report at the Central Memorial Week next Monday. (Central News Agency dispatch from the 21st)

US Ambassador Visits President Wang

[Nanjing] US Ambassador Johnson, accompanied by US Consul General Peck, visited President Wang at the Railway Official Residence at 3:00 PM on the 21st, making his first visit since returning to his post. Wang personally received him, and they spoke for half an hour before he departed. (Special dispatch from the 21st)

[Nanjing] US Ambassador Johnson visited President Wang at the Ministry of Railways Official Residence at 3:00 PM on the 21st, making his first visit since returning to his post. In addition to offering ordinary greetings, they also briefly discussed the recent situation in the United States. The conversation lasted about half an hour before he departed. Wang scheduled a banquet for Johnson at the Ministry of Railways Official Residence at 8:00 PM on the 22nd, and invited over ten people including Beijing US Consul General Peck, Chen Shaokuan, Wang Shijie, Chen Gongbo, Xu Mo, and Tang Youren to accompany them. (Central News Agency dispatch from the 21st)

Joint Meeting of Two Committees of the Legislative Yuan Yesterday

Review and Amend the Stock Exchange Law

[Nanjing] The Legislative Yuan's Legal System and Finance Committees held a joint meeting on the morning of the 21st to review the proposed amendments by Shi Weizhao and others to Articles 31, 42, and 45 of the Stock Exchange Law. Jiao Yitang chaired the meeting. Dai Mingli, section chief of the Currency Department of the Ministry of Finance, attended to explain the results of the review. It is reported that in addition to increasing the margin money for both buyers and sellers, those who violate the provisions of Article 31 will be subject to considerable fines. The opinions have been drafted and submitted to the general meeting for discussion. (Special dispatch from the 21st)

[Nanjing] Mu Ouchu, Chairman of the Shanghai Chinese Cotton Yarn Exchange, arrived in Nanjing on the 21st from Shanghai to negotiate with the Ministry of Finance and the Ministry of Industry for a one-year postponement of transaction taxes and to discuss the issue of cracking down on cotton yarn speculation. Mu said that the request for postponement is likely to be granted. (Special dispatch from the 21st)

[Nanjing] The Commerce Law and Finance Committees of the Legislative Yuan convened a joint meeting on the morning of the 21st to review and amend the Stock Exchange Law. The commissioners spoke at length on the anti-speculation measures of the bill. As a result, Chen Jianru, Shi Weihuan, and Zheng Hongnian were nominated as three commissioners to conduct the review. (Central News Agency dispatch from the 21st)

Mongolian Political Council Scheduled to Hold Second General Assembly

[Beiping] The second general assembly of the Mongolian Political Council is scheduled to be held on March 5th. Except for Kexing'e, Bai Yunti, and Wu Heling, who are in Beijing, and Prince Suo Wang Tuoketuo Hu, who will not be able to attend due to his trip to Wutai Mountain, the rest are preparing to attend. Regarding the various issues of Inner Mongolia, Prince Suo and Xiao Zhenying have been exchanging views in recent days and are in harmonious agreement. Chairman Chiang is also very concerned and frequently sends telegrams to inquire and ask about Prince Suo's health. Xiao Zhenying is acting as a proxy to report everything. Prince Suo will go to Wutai Mountain on the 28th to worship and is expected to stay for a month before returning to Beiping and returning to his Ujimqin banner. (Central News Agency dispatch from the 21st)

President Wang Welcomes Sven Hedin

[Nanjing] President Wang hosted a tea party at the Ministry of Railways auditorium at 5:00 PM on the 21st, inviting ministers and officials above the rank of simplified appointment to welcome Dr. Sven Hedin and request him to lecture on the inspection of the Suiyuan-Xinjiang highway. Over a hundred people attended, including President Wang, Sven Hedin, Ding Weifen, Chen Gongbo, Zhu Jiahua, Huang Musong, Luo Jialun, Zeng Zhongming, Zhang Daofan, Chu Minyi, Peng Xuepei, Zhao Pilian, and councillors and simplified appointment officials from various ministries and commissions. Wang delivered a welcoming speech, stating that Sven Hedin had overcome difficulties and dangers over the past sixteen months, and finally enabled an important field observation on our country's Northwest transportation plan. We admire and thank him for this spirit and difficulty. Then Sven Hedin was invited to give a lecture, first stating his purpose and plan, and then describing the selection and course of the two major Northwest lines. It lasted two hours before it ended. Wang expressed his gratitude and the meeting adjourned at 8:00 PM. (Central News Agency dispatch from the 21st)

Security Commander to be Established in the War Zone

To be concurrently held by the Commissioners of Ji, Mi, Luan and Yu districts.

Zhao Lei's troops to be transferred out of the war zone in three phases.

[Beiping] The exchange of defenses for the war zone security team will be implemented soon. The Second Regiment of Zhao Lei's troops is not in compliance with the prescribed number of people. The provincial government will first send personnel to conduct an inspection to eliminate the weak and retain the strong. After meeting the establishment requirements, it will be transferred to Tongzhou for training at the beginning of next month. Tangshan will be defended by Zhang Tingyu's troops, and Kaiping will be garrisoned by Sun Jizhou's troops for training. The Jilin Province Security Second and Third Brigades Zhou Yuying and Yang Yucheng's troops stationed around Qinhuangdao, Changli, and Haiyang will be transferred out of the war zone and moved to the Qinghe area for training. (Special dispatch from the 21st)

[Tianjin] Zhao Lei returned to Tangshan on the 21st. After discussions in Beiping, his Second Regiment of War Zone Security was reduced to 1,500 men, organized into three brigades, with 500 men per brigade. The excess personnel will be dismissed. Officers will be given ten yuan, and soldiers five yuan. They will be transferred out of the war zone in three phases. Before being trained and reorganized in Tongzhou, Tao Shangming and Zhu Shiqin will inspect and review them. (Special dispatch from the 21st)

[Tianjin] The security team of Zhou Yuying's troops stationed in Changli War Zone, Yang Yucheng's troops stationed in Qian'an, and Fan Jinghe's troops stationed in Jixian, will be transferred to Qinghe in southern Hebei for training after the new security team moves in to exchange defenses. The new war zone security team is being reorganized. The Hebei Provincial Government has internally decided that Zhang Qingyu's troops will be stationed in the Luan district, and Zhang Yantian's troops will be stationed in the Jiaguan district. (Special dispatch from the 21st)

[Beiping] The Yutian Security Team has decided to be transferred back for training when the new security team departs. In addition to the thousand men of Feng Shoupeng's troops, who have been transferred to Zhao Lei's command to be stationed in Tangshan, the rest are planned to be transferred to Tongxian. In the future, a security commander will be established in the war zone, to be concurrently held by the Commissioners of Ji, Mi, Luan and Yu districts. After approval, it can be announced. (Central News Agency dispatch from the 21st)

[Tianjin] The exchange of defenses for the war zone security team has been agreed upon by both China and Japan and will be implemented recently. Zhou Yuying and Yang Yucheng's troops, originally stationed in Changli and Qinhuangdao, will be transferred out of the war zone and moved to the Qinghe area. Zhao Lei's troops, stationed in Tangshan, will be transferred to Tongzhou for exchange of defenses, to be replaced by Zhang Qingyu's troops. Sun Jizhou's troops in Yutian are planned to be transferred to Kaiping. Liu Zuozhou's troops have just resolved the conflict among the teams, and the location of their garrison has not yet been determined. However, the number of troops in each unit is quite large and does not meet the regulations. Before the transfer of defenses, the province will send personnel to inspect and eliminate the old and weak to comply with the establishment. (Central News Agency dispatch from the 21st)

President Wang Holds a Reception for Doihara

[Nanjing] Doihara, accompanied by Koyama Sadakazu, an advisor to the South Manchuria Railway, visited President Wang at the Ministry of Railways Official Residence at 10:00 AM on the 21st in a private capacity. Wang met him after the Central Standing Committee meeting adjourned and returned to his residence. They exchanged pleasantries, and to fulfill his duty as a host to Doihara and Koyama who had come to Beijing for sightseeing from afar, he held a banquet at the official residence at noon to welcome them. Chen Lifu, Zhu Jiahua, Tang Youren, Zeng Zhongming, and Suma, the Japanese consul general in Beijing, were also invited to accompany them. Only ordinary courtesies were exchanged during the banquet, and it adjourned at 2:00 PM. According to Zeng Zhongming, Doihara's visit to President Wang was because he was traveling to Beijing and made a courtesy call. Apart from greetings, he did not mention anything else. Wang's reception for Doihara and others was only to thank them for their visit from afar. (Special dispatch from the 21st)

[Nanjing] Doihara visited President Wang at the Ministry of Railways Official Residence at 10:00 AM on the 21st and made an ordinary visit. They spoke for about twenty minutes before Doihara departed. At 3:00 PM in the afternoon, Doihara and Koyama, an advisor to the South Manchuria Railway, went to the Ministry of Foreign Affairs and other places to bid farewell to Tang Youren and others. Suma returned to Beijing from Shanghai on the morning of the 21st and hosted a banquet for Doihara and others at the Consulate General at 8:00 PM. It is reported that Doihara is scheduled to return to Shanghai by overnight express after Suma's banquet on the evening of the 21st with Koyama. (Central News Agency dispatch from the 21st)

[Nanjing] Doihara left for Shanghai by night train on the 21st. (Special dispatch from the 21st)

Japanese Prepare to Take Over After Illegal Transaction of Chinese Eastern Railway

[Beiping] After the successful sale of the Chinese Eastern Railway, Japan is actively preparing to take over. They have selected 3,000 railway workers from various railways in the Northeast, including 200 senior officials, who were selected by Japan. They arrived in Mu Ling a few days ago and are preparing to depart in batches. (Special dispatch from the 21st)

Liu Guitang's Bandit Troops Invade Near the Great Wall

[Tianjin] Liu Guitang sent his chief of staff, Wang Shichen, to Qian'an, Saheqiao, and Jianchangying to operate, and commanded Liu's bandit mobs lurking along the Great Wall to invade various places south of the Great Wall. The Yutian Security Team of Zunhua County received a letter demanding 50,000 yuan, which was to be sent to Jieshankou by the 26th. The Zunhua Security Team of the Security Team Department, Wang Zhanyuan's troops, therefore mobilized to guard the border. (Special dispatch from the 21st)

[Beiping] Tangshan News, after Liu Guitang rebelled from Chahar, he disturbed the locality and caused great harm. Liu's bandits have not extinguished their ambitions. At the beginning of the month, he and his chief of staff, Wang Shichen, secretly went to Qinhuangdao, and still sent his accomplices to spread orders and gather various groups to gather in the war zone, attempting to rise again. (Special dispatch from the 21st)

Umezu Thanks Song for Sending Personnel to Entertain Him in Chahar

[Tianjin] Song Zheyuan has recovered from his illness and plans to leave Tianjin for Beiping on the 23rd. He will return to Chahar after staying for two days. (Special dispatch from the 21st)

[Tianjin] Umezu, the commander of the Japanese army in Tianjin, visited Chahar and was very impressed. On the 20th, he sent a letter to Song, thanking him for sending personnel to entertain him. (Special dispatch from the 21st)

[Tianjin] Dou Gu arrived at Shanhaiguan on the 20th. After staying for a day and meeting with Garrison Commander Lieutenant Colonel Kawai and Colonel Ochiai, he left for Changchun by train early on the 21st. (Special dispatch from the 21st)

[Beiping] Three members of the Japanese Consulate in Chahar, Shengdao Jiaofang and Ogang Gui, returned to Zhangjiakou from Beiping today. (Special dispatch from the 21st)

Japanese Army in Tianjin Conducts Exercises

[Tianjin] At 10:00 AM today, a company of Japanese infantry in Tianjin conducted street fighting exercises in the Japanese Concession for the visit of Major Okamura and other staff members of the Kwantung Army Headquarters. It ended at 3:00 PM in the afternoon. During the exercises, sandbags were piled up at various street intersections to cut off traffic. (Special dispatch from the 21st)

Sakai, Chief of Staff of the Japanese Army in Tianjin, Visits Beiping

Yin Tong and Others Welcome Him at the Station

[Beiping] Sakai, Chief of Staff of the Japanese Garrison Army in Tianjin, arrived in Beiping from Tianjin tonight. Wakasugi, the chargé d'affaires of the Japanese Embassy, Military Attaché Takahashi, and our representatives Yin Tong, Yin Rugeng, Zhu Shiqin, and others welcomed him at the station. After Sakai got off the train, he went to the Fusang Hotel to stay. He is here on a sightseeing trip and will take the opportunity to visit our military and political authorities. (Special dispatch from the 21st)

[Tianjin] Sakai, Chief of Staff of the Japanese Army in Tianjin, went to Beiping on the 21st to inspect the military. (Special dispatch from the 21st)

[Beiping] Five Japanese military attachés stationed in Tianjin came to Beiping this morning. After getting off the train, they went to the Japanese barracks. (Special dispatch from the 21st)

Japanese Raise the Price of Exit Passports

The Puppet State Restricts the Export of Hard Currency

[Beiping] The Datong Company, established by the Japanese in Yuguan, has been forcibly selling entry permits since January of the 23rd year of the Republic. Anyone leaving the pass from various places inside the pass must purchase one, costing three jiao of silver dollars each. Now the Japanese and puppet authorities are planning to increase the price of the entry permit, charging one silver dollar each, euphemistically called an entry tax, which will be implemented next month. Also, the Japanese recently established a large-scale exchange in Yuguan Station. Anyone entering the pass with merchants who exchange pseudo-currency for hard currency are calculated at 80%. Also, in order to avoid the export of hard currency, the Japanese and puppet authorities, since the implementation of postal services with the Northeast, have issued orders to all post offices that all remittances from the Northeast to within the pass are calculated at 80%. The China Communications and Bank of Liaoning, Jilin and Heilongjiang must also follow this example and must not remit according to the actual number. (Special dispatch from the 21st)

Japanese Monopolize the Red Grain Trade in the Northeast

[Beiping] People from Shenyang talked about how, after the autumn harvest in the Northeast last year, the Japanese widely bought red grain at a price of seven jiao of silver dollars per dou, causing all households to sell out. Now that spring has arrived, the Japanese are forcibly ordering the planting of cotton, which will still be bought by the Japanese after the harvest, causing great panic among farmers. A month ago, the Japanese resold the red grain they had previously bought at a price of more than one yuan and seven jiao per dou. In order to satisfy their hunger, farmers had to buy it, reluctantly. Money is being sucked away by the Japanese. It is said that after the cotton harvest in the Northeast, it will be completely used as raw materials for manufacturing weapons. (Special dispatch from the 21st)

The Executive Yuan Discusses the Shanghai Municipal Government Loan Case

[Nanjing] The Executive Yuan held a review meeting at 9:00 AM on the 21st to discuss the Shanghai Municipal Government's loan of 1 million yuan to build the West Shanghai public housing area. The responsible heads of the Ministry of Finance, the Ministry of Interior, and the Ministry of Health attended. Cai Zengji, Director of the Shanghai Finance Bureau, also attended to explain the plan and process of the case in detail. After discussion, it was considered that it could be established and passed according to the various review opinions, and then submitted to the Executive Yuan meeting for discussion. (Special dispatch from the 21st)

The Ministry of Foreign Affairs Announces Inspectors for Various Provinces

[Nanjing] The Ministry of Foreign Affairs announced Wu Zexiang as the Inspector for Sichuan (stationed in Chongqing), Cheng Jingyuan as the Inspector for Anhui and Jiangxi (stationed in Nanchang), and commissioned Gan Jiehou as the Inspector for Guangdong and Guangxi (stationed in Guangzhou), Yang Guangsheng as the Inspector for Hunan and Hubei (stationed in Hankou). The candidates for the remaining regional inspectors are still being selected. Also, the ministry commissioned former Legislative Commissioner Xie Shoukang as a member of the Treaty Committee. (Special dispatch from the 21st)

Yu Xuezhong Goes to Hankou in Response to Zhang's Telegram

Wan Fulin Accompanies Him

[Beiping] Yu Xuezhong went to Beiping from Tianjin this afternoon in response to Zhang Xueliang's telegram, and went south to Hankou that night. He is scheduled to return north before the end of the month. Yu said that he was going to Hankou in response to a telegram from Zhang, and that Chief of Staff Liu Zhonggan and Guard Captain Zhang, etc. will accompany him. The mission to Hankou will last about a week or so. The details of the mission to Hankou were not described in detail in Zhang's telegram. The current situation of the organization of the North China army will also be discussed. There has been a concrete decision on the issue of the newly compiled security team entering the war zone. The organization of the newly compiled security team is that there are 25 teams under the general team, and the number of people in each team is more than 160 people, but the number of people can be reduced or increased as appropriate. The issue of the security team entering the war zone has been agreed upon, and the exchange of defenses will be carried out once the arrangements are made. Other outstanding matters, such as the takeover of Dongling Malanyu and other outstanding matters, can be resolved in accordance with the established procedures. The Luan County team dispute has been resolved peacefully on the spot and has now come to an end. Through the mediation of Chen Cengshi, the county magistrate of the county, and local officials and gentry, the firearms of the people's group submitted to the security team have been returned, and the assembled people have dispersed. The county has now declared martial law lifted and order has been restored. The leaders of the people's group who started this incident have been sent to the headquarters of the security team for interrogation. Zhao Lei, the commander of the first battalion of Lin Yu, was ordered to come to Beiping to discuss the transfer of defenses of the security team. I once summoned Zhao to inquire about everything. Now Zhao has returned to Tangshan. (Special dispatch from the 21st)

[Tianjin] At 9:10 this morning, Yu Xuezhong, accompanied by Liu Zonggan, Chief of Staff of the 51st Army, Chiang Chunyan, Deputy Officer, and more than ten secretaries and staff members, went to Beiping, and took the Pinghan bus that night to go south to Hankou to meet Vice Zhang. Zhang Houwan, Director of the Department of Civil Affairs, will act as the provincial governor. Wan Fulin also planned to go with Yu to pay a visit to Zhang. (Special dispatch from the 21st)

[Beiping] Wan Fulin went to Hankou tonight in response to Zhang's telegram. (Special dispatch from the 21st)

Sichuan Province Breaks Down Defense Areas

Chiang Praises Generals in Telegram

[Chongqing] Chairman Chiang's telegram to Chairman Liu, Deng Xihou, Tian Songyao, Luo Jitian, and Yang Sen on the 20th said: "Now that the provincial government has been reorganized and established, and the military generals have successively declared that they will break down the defense zones and return the political power, it is enough to see that the worst is over and a new opportunity has arisen, which is very gratifying. However, it is important to implement good deeds and eliminate abuses quickly. I hope that the provincial government and the military generals will properly discuss the method of receiving various garrison areas, submit the report for handover as soon as possible without any hesitation. From now on, the provincial government is responsible for improving politics, and the military generals are dedicated to reorganizing the army. Be diligent in your duties." (Central News Agency dispatch from the 21st)

[Nanjing] Deng Xihou recently sent a telegram to President Wang from Sichuan, saying that the evil system of defense areas in Sichuan has caused years of turmoil. Now, he will return the financial and political affairs of the garrison area to the provincial government, and order the county magistrates of each garrison area to strictly abide by the provincial order in all civil, financial, political, and educational matters. The Political Affairs Committee attached to the military headquarters will also be abolished immediately to clarify the authority and conform to unity. (Central News Agency dispatch from the 21st)

Li's Regiment of the Third Route Army Captures Tianbao Village

[Chongqing] Li Keyuan's regiment of the Third Route Army launched an attack on the bandits from the front of Yinjiapu Gaitou Temple Market on the 19th, and encountered the bandit pseudo-89th Division 266th Regiment in the area of Dabao Liang Yuhuang Temple. Our army advanced bravely and successively occupied the Bidingbei Tianbao Village area and is attacking the Yuhuang Temple. (Central News Agency dispatch from the 20th)

[Fuzhou] After the remnant bandits in eastern Fujian were strictly suppressed by the large army, the bandits' strength was almost completely lost. Shi Honglie ordered his officers and soldiers to actively build bunkers and deploy them in various important passes, and at the same time deployed various elite troops to suppress them step by step in order to achieve complete success. (Central News Agency dispatch from the 21st)

[Hong Kong] Guangdong's income and expenditure are insufficient by one million per month, and it has been decided to reduce military expenditure from 4.2 million per month to 3.5 million from July. (Special dispatch from the 21st)

Murder Case in a Military Man's Home

[Beiping] Sun Guanying, a resident of No. 10 Zhangwang Hutong, Gulou Street, outside Di'anmen, is the director of the 105th Division's office in Beiping, 42 years old, from Jinxi. Because he heard that his second concubine, Jin Xiaoying, had an affair with a coachman named Zhao Lianxiang, he shot and killed Jin with a pistol this morning, and then committed suicide with a gun. His wife, Wang Shuying, immediately notified the wife of Liu Duoquan, commander of the 105th Division, by telephone to come to his home to help with everything. Many important military and political figures went to express their condolences. The coachman and cook were taken to the district for questioning. The court sent personnel to examine the body this afternoon. (Special dispatch from the 21st)

Commentary

The Impact of Germany's Response to the Anglo-French Declaration

— Heng

The Anglo-French London Declaration includes the conclusion of four types of conventions, while also inviting Germany to return to the League of Nations. However, Germany's response only expressed agreement with the conclusion of the sky convention, remaining silent on all other points. What are its intentions? Foreign public opinion is greatly divided. Some say Germany's move aims to disrupt the pace of Britain and France, while others say it intends to create an anti-Russian front. Therefore, international attention is focused on the pivotal role of Britain. If Britain yields to Germany's request and allows Germany to only conclude the sky convention, the pace of Britain and France will inevitably be disrupted, and the situation in Eastern Europe will inevitably return to tension. Therefore, Germany's move contains, to some extent, the above two functions. However, according to yesterday's European dispatches, Britain's attitude is still to firmly adhere to the procedures agreed upon in the Anglo-French London talks on the third of this month, believing that the points discussed by Britain and France are interconnected and cannot be taken in isolation. At the same time, it also politely declined Germany's request for prior Anglo-German negotiations. From this perspective, the pace of Britain and France has not been disrupted by Germany's response. Furthermore, although the Soviet Union is somewhat suspicious of Britain's attitude, Britain has already notified the Soviet Union of the results of the Anglo-French London talks and has also explicitly sought the Soviet Union's views. From this point of view, Britain seems willing to respect the Soviet Union's intentions. Moreover, judging from yesterday's Moscow dispatches, the Soviet Union's attitude is in complete agreement with France, that the maintenance of peace should be holistic rather than partial, and should not favor Western Europe at the expense of Eastern Europe. It can be seen here that not only is the relationship between France and Russia unchanged, but the relationship between Britain and Russia has also not been affected by Germany's response. What is even more noteworthy is that Austrian Chancellor Schuschnigg, due to Germany's failure to abandon its ambitions towards Austria, has also been traveling diligently to visit the French and British authorities in order to consolidate Austria's independence. In view of these points, the role of Germany's response has suffered considerable failure.

As we have said before, Germany's wish seems to be to abandon its ambitions towards Western Europe and retain its freedom of action towards Eastern and Central Europe. Therefore, the peace in its mind is a partial rather than a holistic one. Conversely, for France and Russia, it is holistic rather than partial. The reason why Germany is unwilling to have a holistic peace system is because once such a system is established, Germany will have no way to recover lost territories or expand its territory. Therefore, if Germany were to accept the entirety of the Anglo-French protocol in its position, it would be tantamount to falling entirely into France's diplomatic trap. It is only natural that it cannot but have reservations. As for why France and Russia are eager for a holistic peace, it is because modern warfare often affects the whole body with the slightest movement. If one party is in trouble, the other is in danger of being drawn into the vortex. As in the last World War, which started only with the Austro-Serbian conflict, it was not long before all of Europe was in turmoil. Therefore, they believe that partial peace is not enough to guarantee the peace of all of Europe. Given the intricate complexity of the relations between countries today, the movement of one corner inevitably affects the overall situation. Therefore, to seek peace in terms of specific issues, one should aim for the peace of the whole world. However, at present, European countries are only reluctantly maintaining peace through mutual restraints. Although Germany's response is not enough to destroy this peaceful situation, a truly global peace in Europe can never be achieved by the current situation of horizontal and vertical coordination, mutual restraint, and confrontation.

Britain Watches the Development of the Far East Situation

[London] Foreign Secretary Simon stated today that although Britain is busy negotiating treaties with neighboring countries, it is still paying close attention to developments in the Far East. This statement was made by Simon at the end of a meeting with Guo Taiqi, the Chinese ambassador to Britain. It is said that Guo briefly outlined the recent situation in the Far East. Observers here believe that Britain has invested heavily in China and is therefore deeply concerned about all economic relations in the Far East. (21st National Telegram)

New US Commander of the Asiatic Fleet

[Washington] According to today's order, Rear Admiral Moffett Euport has been appointed as the commander of the United States Asiatic Fleet. He will take office this summer. According to reports, Rear Admiral Moffett organized a mine base in northern Scotland during the European War and commanded it, achieving outstanding results and receiving medals from the US and British governments. He is currently fifty-nine years old. (20th Reuters Telegram)

Wang Chonghui Visits Japanese Prime Minister and Minister of the Army

To Open Up Sino-Japanese Relations

Inquiring About the True Intentions of the Japanese Government and Public

Yesterday Afternoon Banquet for Japanese Dignitaries, Afternoon Visit to Naval Minister Osumi

[Tokyo] Wang Chonghui met with Japanese Foreign Minister Hirota and Vice Minister Shigemitsu on the 20th to exchange views on the issue of Sino-Japanese cooperation. In the evening, he hosted Japanese reporters at the Mingguo Hotel and issued the following statement:

My visit to Japan has neither a formal mission nor do I represent the National Government. During the past six months since returning to China, I have met with people from all walks of life and learned about the general attitude of the Chinese people towards Japan. Therefore, I took this opportunity to come to Japan to convey the attitude of the Chinese side to the Japanese government and public, and at the same time convey the intentions of the Japanese side to China, in order to promote friendship between the two countries. If I must say there is a mission, this is my mission. However, there is nothing else to announce regarding specific issues. (21st Denttsu Telegram)

[Tokyo] At 9:00 a.m. today, Dr. Wang Chonghui visited Prime Minister Okada's official residence. Councillor Ding served as the interpreter. Wang first gave his reasons for coming to Japan, and then stated the following regarding Sino-Japanese cooperation:

In my personal capacity, I am willing to contribute to Sino-Japanese friendship. I intend to meet with famous figures from the Japanese government and public to hear Japan's true intentions regarding concrete strategies for Sino-Japanese diplomatic and economic cooperation, and to reveal the aspirations of the Chinese authorities, with the aim of promoting peace in East Asia. Furthermore, I hope to improve Sino-Japanese relations by establishing peace in the East, and I sincerely hope to resolve various East Asian political and economic issues, etc. Prime Minister Okada thanked Wang for his visit to Japan and said that the Imperial Government would spare no effort to assist Wang's efforts. Wang left after a thirty-minute meeting. (21st Denttsushin Telegram)

[Tokyo] Wang Chonghui continued to meet with Minister of the Army Hayashi this morning for a considerable discussion. Minister Hayashi expressed his views as follows:

China should first stop anti-Japanese words and deeds. Secondly, China's anti-Japanese and insulting behavior is a significant stimulus to Japanese emotions, which has become a major cause of hindering Sino-Japanese cooperation. The main reason for the current state of Sino-Japanese relations is the result of past anti-Japanese and insulting behavior. Anti-Japanese activities in various parts of China or anti-Japanese education for young people seem to have considerable roots. I would like to ask if the Nanjing government has any corrective measures for this situation. Japan, of course, has full sincerity in Sino-Japanese cooperation, and I sincerely hope that your country will first express full sincerity regarding the above points.

Wang Chonghui replied:

It is absolutely not the case that China relies on Europe and the United States to carry out anti-Japanese activities, and there is no such imagination. However, it is inevitable that some people in our country, which has a vast territory, may have such thoughts. China strongly advocates Sino-Japanese cooperation and believes that this is the only path for China. However, there are also various complex situations between China and Japan. We should cooperate with each other to remove the causes. Regarding this point, I hope that your Excellency will give full consideration to it. The National Government is by no means insincere in suppressing anti-Japanese activities, but various things have not been able to come to fruition as soon as possible. Therefore, in order to promote Sino-Japanese cooperation, we are very willing to make sincere efforts, etc. (21st Nichiren Telegram)

[Tokyo] Wang Chonghui visited Naval Minister Osumi at the Navy Ministry at 3:00 p.m. today, accompanied by our embassy in Japan. Wang expressed his desire to promote Sino-Japanese cooperation from the perspective of East Asian peace. Osumi expressed his opinion on this, saying that the way to achieve Sino-Japanese friendship lies in the communication of will. Therefore, he hoped that prominent figures from the Chinese government and public would come to Japan for observation in order to use it as an opportunity for friendship, etc. (21st China United Telegram)

Banquet for Japanese Dignitaries

[Tokyo] Wang Chonghui hosted a grand banquet for more than thirty Japanese dignitaries from various fields at the Imperial Rotary Club at noon on the 21st. The guests included Foreign Minister Hirota, Minister of Communications Tokonami, other cabinet members, Seiyukai President Suzuki, former Minseito President Wakatsuki, Kokumin Domei President Adachi, Director-General of Education Masaki, former Minister of the Army Araki, Navy Admiral Kato Kanji, Bank of Japan President Hijikata, Kangin President Baba, Dr. Oda Yorozu, Vice Foreign Minister Shigemitsu, and other influential figures from the political and business circles, totaling more than thirty people. On the host's side, in addition to Wang himself, the Chinese Ambassador to Japan Jiang Zuobin, Councillor Ding, and others attended. Ambassador Jiang delivered a speech first, followed by Foreign Minister Hirota, who spoke on behalf of the guests. Wang strongly advocated the necessity of Sino-Japanese friendship at the banquet. The grand banquet ended at around 2:00 p.m. After the banquet, Wang visited Naval Minister Osumi at around 3:00 p.m. and had a cordial conversation with him for a long time. (21st Lian Dian)

Talk Pieces with Japanese Reporters

[Tokyo] Dr. Wang met with the press corps yesterday after meeting with the Foreign Minister. The questions and answers are as follows: (Reporter) On what basis do you hope for Sino-Japanese cooperation? (Wang) It is based on Sun Yat-sen's Greater Asianism. However, this requires the two countries to stand on an equal footing and help each other. Regarding this point, I hope that the Japanese government and public will not misunderstand. (Reporter) What are the views of the Chinese side on Sino-Japanese cooperation? (Wang) After returning to China, I have repeatedly met with people from various fields and they all believe that rather than economic cooperation, it is better to restore the Sino-Japanese diplomatic relations, which have been in an abnormal state for the past two or three years, to normalcy. This is a prerequisite. Specifically, first, mutual understanding and recognition between the people of the two countries must be deepened. Second, Sino-Japanese diplomacy, which has been off track for several years, must be restored to normal diplomatic relations. (Reporter) The Japanese side is extremely dissatisfied with China's anti-Japanese and anti-Japanese goods movements and believes that eradicating anti-Japanese actions is a prerequisite for improving Sino-Japanese relations. What is your opinion? (Wang) This can be compared to personal problems. Friendship between two people can be destroyed by one party, but to restore friendship, both parties must approach it with sincerity. The same is true for problems between countries. That is, if the cause of anti-Japanese sentiment can be removed, I believe it will naturally disappear. (Reporter) Foreign Minister Hirota stated in his speech to the current session of the Diet that Japan has absolutely no ambitions towards China, and anti-Japanese sentiment should be stopped immediately. (Wang) If Japan adopts diplomatic policies in accordance with Foreign Minister Hirota's policy, the Sino-Japanese relationship will be easily resolved. (21st Denttsu Telegram)

Hirota Explains His Aspirations for Diplomacy with China

Working Hard to Adjust Sino-Japanese Relations

Aiming to Achieve Peaceful Cooperation Between the Two Countries

[Tokyo] Japanese Foreign Minister Hirota stated in the Diet today in response to questions about his China policy that he is currently working hard to sort out Sino-Japanese relations, with the aim of maintaining peace in the East through closer cooperation between the two countries. Fortunately, foreign countries are now gradually understanding Japan's true intentions in the Far East. Personally, he has great trust in Chiang Kai-shek. If his belief is wrong, the peace of the East may be overturned, but he is working to sort out Sino-Japanese relations with this unshakable belief, in order to finally achieve closer cooperation between the two countries for peace in the East. (21st Reuters Telegram)

[Tokyo] Foreign Minister Hirota answered the questions of Representative Haruhiko Sohara of the Kokumin Domei in the House of Representatives Budget Committee on his aspirations for diplomacy with China as follows:

It has been a year and a half since I took office as Foreign Minister, and I have not yet started on the China issue. This is a fact. I feel that if Japan is eager to misunderstand China, I am deeply concerned that this will create such a result. Therefore, I first carried out diplomatic work with countries other than China, and postponed China until later. If I am unable to remain as Foreign Minister at the time of the cabinet change, it is possible that my lifelong wish for thorough diplomacy with China will end without being started. Fortunately, today Japan's true intentions have been understood by various countries. I have no doubts about my attitude towards Chiang Kai-shek. If all my beliefs are wrong, the peace of the East will be overturned. There are also rumors about my beliefs among Chinese dignitaries, and for the sake of peace in the East, I should ask for cooperation. (21st Nichiren Telegram)

[Tokyo] Representative Haruhiko Sohara raised a question on cultural undertakings in China in the House of Representatives. Foreign Minister Hirota answered as follows:

In the future, more attention should be paid to cultural facilities in China. So far, there are only a few facilities north of the Yangtze River. In the future, we also plan to seek practical ways to handle the Guangdong area. (21st Nichiren Telegram)

Japan Refreshes Diplomatic Lineup to Cope with Extraordinary Times

Dividing Regions and Convening Envoy Conferences

East Asia Under the Direct Guidance of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs

[Tokyo] Foreign Minister Hirota, because the Japanese government is in an international extraordinary period, has decided to use a compromise diplomacy based on the principle of non-aggression and non-threat to deal with the international community. He sent Ambassador Yoshida to visit overseas embassies and recently decided to send Ambassador Matsushima to the countries of Asia Minor to seek contact. His preparations for all aspects are steadily underway. As diplomatic affairs have become increasingly complex and important year by year, the Ministry of Foreign Affairs and the overseas embassies' instruction-based diplomacy has not been able to be thorough, and the Diplomatic Efficiency Committee is currently planning to convene one or two joint conferences of ambassadors and ministers every year starting next year in the politically important areas of Europe and the commercially important areas of Central and South America to study fundamental diplomatic policies. The necessary expenses are planned to be included in the Showa 11th year budget. It is reported that the specific contents of the plan are as follows: (1) The venue for the European regional ambassadors' conference will be Paris, France. (2) The venue for the Central and South American regional conference will be Rio de Janeiro, the capital of Brazil. (3) East Asian regions such as China and Southeast Asia will be directly guided by the Ministry. (4) The US region will be convened by the Embassy in the United States to hold consul general and consular conferences at any time. (21st Nichiren Telegram)

Kengo Adachi Questions Diplomacy

[Tokyo] The center of the Diet has now shifted to the House of Peers budget meeting. The meeting was held at 10:00 a.m. this morning. Former Foreign Minister Kengo Adachi, the most authoritative figure in the House of Peers on foreign administrative affairs, questioned diplomatic issues. Because of the importance of the issue, it was held as a closed-door meeting and no eavesdropping was allowed. The questions asked by Yoshizawa are as follows:

(1) Border security between Russia and Manchukuo is becoming more serious. We do not believe that Russia has any intention of war. Does the government intend to conclude a non-aggression treaty with Russia? (2) To establish peace in the Far East, we should maintain close relations with the United States, but there is a difference in the degree to which this is done. What is the government's view on this? (3) The anti-Japanese issue in Arizona, USA, is of great importance to the resolution of the issue in relation to US-Japan diplomacy. What methods does the Foreign Minister intend to use to resolve this issue? (21st Nichiren Telegram)

Yoshida Returns Home After Inspecting Europe and the United States

[Tokyo] Yoshida Shigeru, the diplomatic inspector who was specially commissioned by Foreign Minister Hirota to visit Europe and the United States, returned home on the Asama Maru this morning. He is scheduled to visit Foreign Minister Hirota immediately to report the results of the inspection. The content of his advice will be to request a refresh of the diplomatic lineup. (21st Denttsu Telegram)

Matsushima Will Be Dispatched to the Near East

[Tokyo] In order to open up new markets in Asia Minor and to contact consulates in Southeast Asia and the Dutch East Indies, Foreign Minister Hirota has decided to send former Ambassador to Italy Matsushima Hajime to Annam, Siam, India, Persia, Afghanistan, and other countries. Ambassador Matsushima will leave Japan in late April and is scheduled to travel for three months. (21st Nichiren Telegram)

Singapore Solidifies Defense

Naval Base Promoted to Completion

— The Governor of Malaya's Expression —

If he can maintain influence over this matter for a long time, he will not let go. (20th Reuters Telegram)

French House of Representatives Maritime Committee Calls for Adding Warships

One Vessel of 35,000 Tons

[Paris] The House of Representatives Maritime Committee today passed a resolution advocating the inclusion of the construction of a 35,000-ton warship in the 1935 French shipbuilding program. This resolution asks the French government to submit a naval program as soon as possible and recommends that this program should stipulate the construction of two new destroyers, each of 1,700 tons. (20th Reuters Telegram)

US Congressman Suggests Setting Up a World Spy Network

[Washington] According to the bill submitted to Congress today by California Democratic Congressman Duckweiler, the United States will set up a spy network all over the world. Duckweiler claimed that Japanese spies, disguised as fishermen, were scouting the movements of the US fleet during the Pacific maneuvers. He asked for an increase in the US Army's budget for the purpose of setting up spies. In the event of a conflict between Japan and the United States, Japan has already stationed a small army in California, which can launch an attack on the United States at any time. To cope with this crisis, the United States should consolidate the defense of the West Coast to a considerable extent. After a recent congressional committee investigated the propaganda and espionage work carried out by foreign governments in the United States for several days, it issued a report requesting funds to set up a spy network, which followed this report. The committee's report stated that Soviet Russia had failed to fulfill its promise to stop communist propaganda in exchange for diplomatic recognition. Germany, Italy, and Mexico were also spreading propaganda. Members of the investigative committee believe that the activities of foreign spies within the United States are a clear threat to democracy. Political observers here say that the United States' only spy system is the intelligence office of the Army and Navy, which is well known. The government generally opposes the adoption of a spy system, believing that this is a provocative plan in peacetime and is unnecessary. (20th National Telegram)

US Navy Chief Opposes Rebuilding Airships

Saying They Are Not Suitable for Military Use

[Washington] Secretary of the Navy Swanson declared today that he intends to oppose the US Navy's rebuilding of airships, which are useful for commerce, but not suitable for military use. Swanson's statement was made in light of the loss of the US airship Macon in the Pacific Ocean eight days ago. The airship cost US$2.45 million to build. The US Navy had a total of three airships, and they have all been lost. (20th Reuters Telegram)

Roosevelt Sends Message to Congress Asking to Extend the National Recovery Act

[Washington] President Roosevelt strongly advocated today that the National Recovery Act be extended for two years, but it is said that under this act, monopolies have been established, which have harmed industries and operators. Therefore, it is not certain whether President Roosevelt's efforts will be successful. The Senate Judiciary Committee will investigate the accusations against the monopoly system, and the Senate Finance Committee will also investigate the matter. Many Democratic members of Congress are dissatisfied with the effects of the recovery plan. Therefore, even though the Democratic Party has a majority in both houses of Congress, this bill may not be easily passed in both houses. President Roosevelt sent a message to Congress asking that the National Recovery Act be extended for two years without changing its fundamental purpose and principles. President Roosevelt said that the recovery plan has achieved its recent goal, which is to curb the downward trend of the recession and encourage the people to move forward. Child labor, which has long been criticized, has now been abolished. Factories that oppress workers have now been eliminated, and millions of wage earners are no longer suffering from the pain of low wages, unsustainable living, and excessive work. More importantly, the business community itself has clearly recognized the advantages of cooperation and self-control, and the need to end unstable financial and unfair habits in patriotism. The principles of the recovery plan are very sound. If these principles are abandoned, the harassment of industries will be revived. If industries cannot automatically fall within this scope, the government must have the unquestionable power to establish the minimum standards of fair competition, and the right of employees to organize themselves for collective bargaining must be fully protected. The rights of monopoly and private pricing systems in industries, especially in the oil, coal, and gas industries, cannot be allowed to exist. The American people need the government to supervise these industries in order to avoid waste and control their production, and to crack down on price-cutting competition and excessive profits. However, care must be taken to prevent the cooperative privileges that prevent unfair competition from turning into franchise systems that destroy fair competition. (20th Reuters Telegram)

Hoover Advocates Restoring the Gold Standard

[Tucson] Former President Hoover declared today that the United States should immediately restore the gold standard, thereby restoring the people's confidence in the dollar. The attitude of foreign countries can be ignored. Regarding the gold bond case, Hoover said that the judges of the Supreme Court clearly believed that the government's failure to pay public debt in gold was unconstitutional. The majority of people conclude that the people cannot resist this unconstitutional act. The current need is to restore the credit of the dollar. The present opportunity is suitable for restoring the credit of the dollar. All fears of future depreciation should be discarded. If we want to help the recovery of the poor, we should make the dollar exchange for gold based on the current market price of five dimes and nine cents. We do not have to wait for other countries before restoring the gold standard and the credit of the currency. Sooner or later, they will follow us to restore the gold standard. Foreigners fear our actions more than they fear our management of the currency because the latter will put us at a disadvantage. Hoover added that restoring the gold standard would have the following three results: (1) Reduce unemployment more than other steps. (2) Restore the activity of production tools. (3) Curb inflation. (20th National Telegram)

British Trade Deficit

[London] The Department of Commerce officially announced today that Britain's foreign trade in 1934 had a trade deficit of £1 million, compared with a trade surplus of £2 million in 1933. However, compared with the trade deficit of £51 million in 1932, there was still a lot of progress last year, so it is still possible to be happy. The Department of Commerce estimates that the income from British foreign investment was £175 million last year, £160 million in 1931, and £150 million in 1932. (20th National Telegram)

Korean Revolutionary Leader Ahn Chang-ho Released After Serving Sentence

Arrested for the Hongkou Bombing Case

More Than Four Thousand People Welcome Him at the Train Station

Pyongyang News: Ahn Chang-ho, the leader of the Korean Revolutionary Party, was arrested and imprisoned in Shanghai by the Japanese authorities two years ago. He was released from Daejeon Prison on the 11th of this month and was escorted by relatives and friends to his hometown of Pyongyang. There were more than 4,000 people welcoming him, and the area around the train station was packed. Because he could not shake hands with everyone, he stood high on the car, and everyone was happy to see the demeanor of the old revolutionary. Some were even moved to tears. It is reported that Ahn has been running for the revolution since he was a teenager. When Korea was亡, he fled overseas and engaged in the independence movement. San Francisco and Los Angeles in the Americas, and Shanghai and Beiping in China were all centers of activity for the man. After the January 28th Hongkou bombing case, Ahn was arrested by a member of the Japanese consulate at a friend's house in Baokangli on Avenue Joffre in Shanghai and then transported to the capital court of the country, where he was sentenced to four years in prison. Because of the pardon of the birth of the Japanese prince, the term was shortened, so it was possible to return to his hometown after twenty-six years. (World News Agency)

Opening of Chinese Painting Exhibition in London

[London] The Chinese Ancient and Modern Art Exhibition opened today at the New Burlington Galleries by the wife of the Chinese Ambassador, Guo Taiqi. The exhibition features 230 famous paintings, accompanied by a beautifully printed catalog containing Ambassador Guo's preface, a commentary by Laurence Binyon, a renowned author and authority on Eastern art, and a brief history of Chinese painting written by Liu Haisu. The chairman of the special committee assisting in the establishment of the exhibition, Sir Harry F. Fox, was unable to attend due to official commitments and sent a letter of apology, stating that "we can now appreciate representative works of the new era of Chinese painting, and then contemplate the spirit of Chinese art throughout the ages. This is a sign of the growing friendship between China and Britain. We now feel that the East may have teachings worth listening to for the West." Ambassador Guo addressed the guests, saying that the collected works "show that China, amidst revolutionary changes, still maintains the spirit of its ancient art. The progress of Chinese artistic creation is boundless, just like the creative power displayed by the Chinese people in all aspects of their national and personal lives. If our British friends appreciate these paintings with sympathy, they can gain a deeper understanding of the emotions and thoughts of the Chinese people. Thus, those who organized this exhibition can be said to have not worked in vain and have gained much." After Ambassador Guo's speech, the guests began to view the exhibits and praised the works one after another. Today, The Times published a detailed report on the exhibition, saying that "this exhibition is a delightful experience. Each painting is full of poetic meaning, excelling in spirit. The brushstrokes are bold and do not seek delicacy, and the style varies according to the nature of the painter." (Reuters, 21st)

Shanghai Waterworks Engineer Suddenly Disappears En Route to England

Slippers Found on Deck, Presumed to Have Fallen into the Sea

[London] Mr. Stringer, a British engineer with the Shanghai Waterworks, who was on leave returning home, disappeared today on the Vienna steamer from Hook of Holland, Netherlands, to Harwich, England. Mr. Stringer had two companions on board, one of whom shared a cabin with him. When the ship was about two hours away from Harwich, Mr. Stringer suddenly disappeared. He was only wearing shorts, and a pair of slippers was found on deck. Mr. Stringer is presumed to have fallen into the sea. (Havas, 20th)

Cuban Students Stage Mass Strike

Support University Students Demanding Civil Rights

Havana The educational center of Cuba today held a mass strike. 125,000 public school students and 3,000 teachers went on strike to support university students. University students voted on Monday to support an indefinite strike. It is estimated that about 25,000 higher education students have joined the university strike. The crux of the situation is that university students are demanding the restoration of civil liberties and the disarming of the police. Liberal students have repeatedly protested to the military and police authorities, and the situation has gradually become serious. On Monday, it evolved into collective action. The government and military authorities acknowledged the public's opinion and expressed sympathy with the striking students, and are now on special alert to prevent any incidents after the student strike. President Mendieta announced that last week, the Communists started an incident and threw bricks at the British Consulate. There were as many as 50 bombs exploded in the streets of Havana. The government's initial intention to set up armed police was to prevent similar incidents. It is said that student leaders oppose the military government and do not want to attend classes until the republican government and civil rights are restored. (National Telegram, 20th)

Annual Report of British Silver Company

[London] Samuel Montagu & Co. today released a substantial annual report, stating that the events of the past year have largely eliminated the instability regarding the trend of silver. U.S. legislation is a significant factor in the improvement of silver prices. The United States still needs more than 110 million ounces of silver, which seems predictable, but everything depends on the state of its purchases. In the absence of new developments, and based on recent experience, silver prices, even if not solid, can be guaranteed to remain stable for some time to come. It also said that in 1934, the world produced 180 million ounces of new silver, compared to 164 million ounces in 1933. At first glance, the rise in silver prices and the progress of the situation have not had much impact. However, it should be noted that silver is mostly a byproduct, and since the demand for low-grade metals containing silver is not abundant, the output of silver will naturally not increase sharply. (Reuters, 20th)

"Nichikasamaru" Fully Loaded with Iron Ore from Daye Mine Sinks After Collision

Wakamatsu The Mitsui & Co.-owned ship "Nichikasamaru" (2,800 tons), fully loaded with iron ore for ironmaking from Daye, China, arrived at Wakamatsu Port at 5:30 this morning. En route, it collided head-on with the Tatsuma Kisen-owned "Gochikumaru" (5,000 tons) off the coast of Ichinose outside the port. The "Nichikasamaru" sank immediately, killing one first-class cook and seriously injuring one other. The remaining crew members were rescued by a rescue ship. (Dentsu Telegram, 21st)
