Italian Supreme Defense Committee Decides on Wartime Self-Sufficiency

Nationwide Industrial Mobilization Ordered

Efforts to Seek Economic Independence

Military Measures to be Taken Against Abyssinia

More Than 10,000 Troops Awaiting Dispatch

Rome The Supreme Defense Committee recently held four meetings, which have now concluded. A communique was released today, detailing the possibility of Italian self-sufficiency in wartime. The communique stated that the Supreme Defense Committee has completed all tasks, prepared to take necessary measures in a timely manner, so that if Italy is provoked by other countries, it can stand undefeated. The Committee also studied the production sources of various necessities in the event of an emergency, and formulated a plan to directly control the production and consumption of these necessities in times of crisis. (Havas, 20th)

Rome The Supreme Defense Committee issued a communique yesterday detailing the possibility of Italian self-sufficiency in wartime. The issuance of this communique is the first time in the 13 years of Fascist rule. The reason for this announcement is to reassure the people in response to their concerns. This is the same as the Fascist Supreme Council issuing a communique explaining Italy's military preparations in the event of danger in Europe. The announcement by the Supreme Defense Committee is specifically for civilian mobilization. As for military mobilization, it has been proceeding according to plan, as can be seen from the mobilization of reservists from the 1911 class. The prevention of poison gas has been specifically studied, and the results have been displayed at exhibitions in various places. The communique issued yesterday by the Supreme Defense Committee lists various substitutes. This list of substitutes was compiled and produced by the National Research Council under the guidance of the great scientist Marconi. This research is sufficient to prove Italy's efforts to seek economic independence. Italy has decided to reduce the import of foreign goods. This decision has forced Italian industries to find the raw materials they need domestically, without relying on foreign countries. Furthermore, the order restricting the quantity of imports is effectively closing Italy's doors, preventing most foreign products from entering. This order can be seen as a mobilization of Italian industry. The conditions set by this order are so strict that if Italian industry can operate normally, the Supreme Defense Committee's claim that "Italy can be self-sufficient in wartime" can be absolutely proven in fact. (Havas, 20th)

Naples, Italy Italy considers Abyssinia's disregard for its war preparations to be unacceptable and will soon send another 15,000 troops to Italian Somaliland to urge it to reconsider. 3,000 troops have already set sail to join the Italian army on the front lines. The Italian government has openly expressed its displeasure at Abyssinia's neglect of this move. The troops conscripted this time to serve in East Africa are said to be the Misenna combat brigade. Official sources claim that these troops will depart by the end of this week, at the latest by March 1st. It is understood that Mussolini's purpose in sending more troops is to assert national prestige and force Abyssinian officials to submit. Meanwhile, news from the Abyssinian capital claims that Abyssinian leaders remain indifferent to the Italo-Abyssinian conflict. Abyssinia has stated that it will only follow the orders of the League of Nations. Abyssinia has dispatched elite troops to the mountainous areas to defend against an Italian attack. Since the deployment of additional Italian troops, the Italian front has not been attacked by Abyssinian bandits. The League of Nations Committee, which is currently meeting in the Abyssinian capital, declares that this incident can be resolved peacefully and that neither Italy's provocative attitude nor Abyssinia's indifference will cause any problems. (National Telegram, 21st)

Austro-French Diplomatic Talks

Non-Interference Pact as Main Topic

[Paris] Austrian Chancellor Schuschnigg and Foreign Minister Berger-Waldenegg, who are visiting France, departed last night. Le Matin reports, "The Austro-French talks will focus on the plan for a Central European non-interference pact. This pact emphasizes the transformation of the Danube River region. If it succeeds, the situation in Central Europe will surely return to tranquility." (Havas, 21st)

Vienna Before departing for France, Chancellor Schuschnigg gave a statement to a Havas News Agency representative: "We will not allow any infringement on the political system currently adopted by Austria, as this system is of great benefit to normalizing the situation in the Danube River region and even Europe." The Chancellor continued, saying that his government is a faithful successor to the policies set by former Chancellor Dollfuss, both in domestic and foreign affairs. (Havas, 20th)

Vienna Austrian Chancellor Schuschnigg and Foreign Minister Berger-Waldenegg departed for Paris and London last night at 8:10 PM, hoping for stronger international support for Austria's anti-German movement. Like Italy, Britain and France deeply desire that Austria not be invaded by the political and territorial ambitions of the Hitlerites. It is understood that Schuschnigg and Berger-Waldenegg intend to clearly inquire of the British and French foreign ministers what attitude the two countries will take if the National Socialists attempt to overthrow the Austrian government again. Austria's future depends on the answers of the two countries. If the Austrian government can rely on the military and financial assistance of Italy, France, and Britain, it can continue to resist Germany. Otherwise, it will have to make peace with Germany. Since the return of the Saar, the National Socialists have intensified their activities in Austria. As soon as the results of the Saar plebiscite were announced, Austria was filled with National Socialist propaganda, demanding that Austrians also vote for self-determination. Although the current government is fighting hard, it cannot appeal to either the left or the right, because it banned both the Socialist and Communist parties last February. Therefore, the government is unwilling to hold general elections immediately. If Schuschnigg and Berger-Waldenegg succeed in this trip, they will not need to appease other parties and will continue to build a Catholic group state, completing the work of former Chancellor Dollfuss. Another background of this negotiation is the restoration of the Habsburg dynasty. It is well known that Schuschnigg is an enthusiastic monarchist, but due to international relations, he still believes that it is not yet the time to talk about restoration. Observers say that his mention of this is because the major European powers and the Little Entente have not yet agreed to recall Archduke Otto. Therefore, Schuschnigg will inquire of Britain and France this time to gauge whether the time is ripe to make Czechoslovakia and Yugoslavia no longer object. Schuschnigg's reason for restoration is that the Austrian people mostly want restraint. Therefore, if Otto ascends the throne, the National Socialist movement will die out. Another issue to be discussed with France is the Rome Protocols. Austria is certainly very grateful for this agreement, but if Germany is unwilling to sign, it will ultimately be ineffective. As for the London Agreement, Austria will also request the cancellation of the treaty's restriction on the army of 30,000 men. It is likely that Schuschnigg will request that informal troops, such as the Catholic Vanguard and the Home Guard, be merged into the formal army, and Britain and France will give this sympathetic consideration. (National Telegram, 21st)

Formal Note Clarifying Position to Britain, France, Soviet Russia

Formation of East European Mutual Assistance Pact

As a Condition for Participating in the Air Defense Agreement

[Moscow] The French Ambassador to the Soviet Union, Alphand, delivered a note to the Soviet People's Commissar for Foreign Affairs, Litvinov, stating that after French Prime Minister Flandin and Foreign Minister Laval consulted with the British government authorities in London and concluded the London Agreement, the British and French governments wished to know the Soviet government's views on the purpose of the above-mentioned agreement. On February 19th, the British Ambassador to the Soviet Union, Chilston, also sent a letter to Litvinov, expressing the same opinion. The Soviet government yesterday instructed its ambassadors to Britain and France to deliver a reply to the respective governments as follows:

"The announcement issued after the London Conference stated that this agreement 'aims to strengthen the cooperation between European countries to consolidate world peace' and at the same time 'to curb tendencies that could promote war.' The Soviet government expresses its welcome to this statement. The Soviet government has long held that in the current situation, since thorough disarmament cannot be achieved and supervision and restriction of armaments are also difficult, the only way to prevent international warfare is to conclude regional mutual assistance pacts between countries that genuinely wish to eliminate war. The Soviet government is delighted to learn that the British and French authorities have stipulated the conclusion of a pact to guarantee the security of European countries (especially the most vulnerable areas). At the same time, the London Conference has made further progress by stipulating that if a country is attacked in the circumstances stipulated in the pact, other countries will immediately provide assistance. The Soviet government believes that in the current situation, if war breaks out in Europe, it cannot be confined to one corner. Therefore, the Soviet government believes that under this unified plan involving all parts of Europe, we must recognize that mutual dependence is essential to preserve the security of the entire continent. Therefore, the Soviet government believes that the realization of the London Conference's goal of organizing European security must wait until all the various regional agreements and arrangements listed in the London announcement are fully realized. Conversely, if any of these agreements are neglected, not only will the purpose of 'consolidating the hope of peace' not be achieved, but the peace within the territories concerned will also be encouraged to be destroyed. The Soviet government is willing to believe that the drafters of this announcement also hold such thoughts. At the same time, the regional pacts that have been discussed by several countries before the London consultations will not only not be damaged, but will also receive new support from the London Agreement. After the conclusion of the London Agreement, we can say that the four major European powers, namely the Soviet Union, France, Britain, and Italy, as well as the Little Entente and the Balkan Entente countries, all agree with the idea that the most urgent and effective steps must be taken at present, using the method of mutual assistance pacts, to contain military aggression. The above-mentioned countries have a total population of 365 million, accounting for 70% of the total European population. At the same time, other European countries are also sympathetic to steps to consolidate peace. Therefore, those with tendencies to promote the current war crisis are in the minority. In such a situation, who would believe that the vast majority of European countries, working together to strive for peace, cannot complete the task of consolidating peace with the necessary means? The Soviet government welcomes the London Agreement under the condition that it is fully and indivisibly implemented in the spirit stated above and eagerly hopes that it will be implemented in its entirety with a firm spirit." (TASS, 21st)

British Cabinet Resolves to Convey to the French Foreign Ministry

Whether to Respond to the Russian Note Awaits Consultation

Negotiation Process Will Precede Germany and then Russia

[Paris] The decision of the British Cabinet has been formally conveyed to Foreign Minister Laval, which has aroused heated discussions and various speculations in the local newspapers. Some newspapers believe that Britain will raise certain questions to Germany to determine the true meaning shown in the German reply. However, most newspapers unanimously praise the British government's impartial attitude in handling the various issues in the Anglo-French declaration, as these issues are inherently interrelated and cannot be divided. However, the London attitude is considered to be quite cautious regarding Simon's visit to Berlin. As for the Russian note to France, the local newspapers especially consider it a major contribution to peace. L'Avenir believes that although the atmosphere of Anglo-French coordination and Anglo-Russian rapprochement is good, the future attitude of Britain is still uncertain. However, if Germany is unwilling to comply, Britain's attitude will not go beyond two paths: one is that Britain insists on its position in the Anglo-French declaration, and the other is to allow France to seek other means of mutual assistance. If it is the former, Germany's position will naturally become more difficult. According to the newspaper's observation, Britain seems to be taking the former path. (National Telegram, 21st)

[London] Regarding the Anglo-French declaration of the two countries in London, according to a semi-official report from the Russian side, it is best to visit Moscow, or even Warsaw, after the British cabinet members go to Berlin. Well-informed sources here believe that if Moscow formally invites the British government, Britain will clearly express its approval. As for the British cabinet members going to Warsaw, no news has been received as of yet. In addition, as to whether to respond to the notes from Soviet Russia and Anglo-France, London believes that it should be jointly agreed with Paris. If it is believed that a response should be given, it should be agreed whether to respond jointly or separately. In short, the notes sent by the Soviet Russian ambassadors to Britain and France to the respective governments yesterday are extremely welcome to well-informed sources here. (Havas, 21st)

Anglo-French Views are the Same

[Paris] Today, the British Cabinet decided that the items recommended in the Anglo-French declaration of February 3rd are closely related. If the Anglo-German talks only select one item from the recommendations for discussion, it would be meaningless. French political figures are very satisfied with this decision of Britain, believing that this explanation of the British Cabinet is completely consistent with the French point of view. The governments of Britain and France will now make close contact through normal diplomatic channels. The visit of British Foreign Secretary Simon to Paris on February 28th is particularly important. In addition, political circles are focusing on the reply to Germany, as the previous German reply to the Anglo-French government's note did not address the Danube River Agreement, the East European Mutual Assistance Agreement, and Germany's return to the League of Nations. The British government's reply to Germany will inevitably inquire further in order to determine Germany's attitude towards these issues. (Havas, 20th)

Britain is Concerned About Two Things

[London] Regarding the issues arising from the Anglo-French declaration of February 3rd, it has been rumored that the British government has made representations to the Soviet Russian ambassador to Britain, and at the same time, the British ambassador to Russia has also consulted with the Soviet Russian government. According to well-informed sources, this statement is untrue. After the London talks, although the British ambassador to the Soviet Union exchanged views with the Soviet Russian government, this was the same as the statements made by British diplomatic representatives to other governments, merely delivering the Anglo-French declaration of February 3rd and giving verbal explanations to ensure that there would be no ambiguity about the intentions of this declaration, especially regarding the interconnectedness of the items recommended by Anglo-France, making detailed explanations. Apart from this, Britain has no other dealings with the Soviet Russian government. Well-informed sources also said that Britain's attitude towards Soviet Russia is concerned with nothing more than two things: one is that Britain is directly concerned only with Western Europe, while Britain does not assume the main task in Eastern Europe; the other is that Britain wants to give Moscow the feeling that Britain not only does not want to reduce Russia's security status, but also Britain is advising Germany to conclude mutual assistance pacts with its neighbors, with the intention of making Russia secure. (Havas, 20th)

Changyuan Floodwaters Have Not Receded

[Tianjin] Changyuan County Magistrate Zhang Qinglu telegraphed the province that the western end of the Zhengba embankment of the Guantai closure project was once in danger on the 16th due to the rapid current. However, it was turned into safety after intensive rescue efforts throughout the night. Currently, the breach has not been closed, and the water depth is 14 meters. Hemp bags and straw are needed. The county magistrate also telegraphed that the floodwaters surrounding the city have not receded, and only one main street in the inner city has not been invaded by water. If the floodwaters recede recently, spring plowing will be possible. However, there is a shortage of cash, and it is planned to organize rural loans for relief. The province instructed the Yellow River Disaster Relief Association to inquire about the amount of funds needed and the number of arable acres in order to verify and handle the matter. Reuters Special Business Intelligence Telegraph, February 21

Gold and Silver

London Gold Price: Today is 142 shillings and 11 pence, 3 and a half pence higher than yesterday.

London Silver: The difference between the spot silver market and futures today is not significant. The spot price rose 0.0625 to 25 pence and 1875. Futures remained unchanged at 25 pence and 25. US and Chinese buyers bought in the morning, while Indian and speculators both bought and sold. Market sentiment was stable at the close.

Exchange Rates

British-American: The London foreign exchange market fluctuated slightly this morning. Demand for gold coins rose slightly, but the exchange rate was not affected. The opening price for British-American exchange was $4.88625, 0.125 lower than the British-American closing price yesterday. It gradually fell, and at 1:00 PM, the price was $4.881875, 0.4375 lower than the opening price. However, at 2:00 PM, it rebounded 0.125 to $4.883125.

British-French: The opening price was 73 francs 81, 2 pounds lower than yesterday's closing price. It rose 1 pound at 11:00 AM, fell 6 pounds at 12:00 PM to 73 francs 76, and then rebounded 3 pounds to 73 francs 79 at 2:00 PM.

Cotton and Wheat

New York Cotton: The cotton market opened today with some prices unchanged and some down 2 pounds. The plan for currency inflation is uncertain, so the cotton market opened slightly lower today. There was not much trading, but inquiries from the industry were good. Europe also expressed interest, and sellers were not very numerous, so it is expected that prices may rise today.

Chicago Wheat: The wheat market opened slightly higher today, but prices fluctuated very little within an hour of opening, similar to the situation in the cotton market.

Liverpool Wheat: In the wheat market today, the price for May futures at 1:00 PM was 4 shillings, 10 pence, and 875, the same as yesterday's closing price.

Liverpool Cotton: Cotton prices were weak today. At 1:00 PM, May futures were sold for 6 pence 82, 2 pounds lower than yesterday's closing price.

Rubber

London: The market was very quiet today. The transaction price for July-September futures at noon was 6 pence 6875, with no change from the closing price of the previous day.

New York: Market prices rose slightly today, with March futures up 4 pounds.

Securities

New York: The stock market did not have any new excitement this morning, so the market situation was mixed again. Most stocks fell slightly at the opening, with public utility, railway, and oil stocks all under pressure. Loew's opened down 0.75 to 33.75, but the opening decline mostly turned into a rise within the first hour. At 10:45, the price of Loew's stock returned to 34.125. Japan's Economic Strategy (Dalian Correspondence)

Realizing the Japan-"Manchukuo" Economic Alliance

Forming a Superior Position in the Far East

The idea of consolidating the Japan-"Manchukuo" economic alliance has been advocated for a long time, but it has not been fully realized. The reason is that order has not yet been restored within the four northeastern provinces, and economic construction cannot naturally enter the right track. At the same time, there are still various unresolved problems in Japan. Regarding the order in the Northeast, it doesn't matter much. As long as the areas along the railway can maintain their normal state, it can be muddled through, and there is no fear of other troubles. And the social and economic contradictions in Japan have a small impact on the four northeastern provinces. However, the disunity of civil and military affairs in politics will almost directly reflect back. For example, Japanese capitalists have finally encountered a golden age in the past three years, but the total amount of investment in the four northeastern provinces in recent years has been no more than 350 million yen. (This is still the nominal capital amount, and the actual amount is even less than this).

This number is probably less than half of the military expenditure in the past three and a half years. So why are they unwilling to invest? It is because the power of the military is rising, especially in the areas under the jurisdiction of the Kwantung Army. They are even more suspicious and fear that if something happens, their property will not receive definite political protection, so they are always hesitant and dare not easily invest in the four eastern provinces, but only try their best to expand their import and export trade.

After the Kwantung Army's control method was changed from three-in-one to two-in-one between the military and the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, the power of capitalists became even smaller and they had to obey the orders of the military commander. Although they are very dissatisfied, they can't do anything about it. Now, the controlled economy, and the co-existence and co-prosperity of Japan and "Manchukuo" are the controlled economy commanded by the military, and the co-existence and co-prosperity under the military sword. We can understand its content by looking at the outline of the Japan-"Manchukuo" Economic Joint Committee Treaty to be implemented in March this year.

'1. The Government of Japan and the Government of "Manchukuo" shall, in order to ensure the strengthening of industrial and economic control between the two countries, recognize the control and uniqueness of the economic division of the two countries, with the premise of not causing drastic changes in the other country's business organization, and for the purpose of jointly establishing a national standard policy, establish the Japan-"Manchukuo" Economic Joint Committee in Changchun.

'2. The composition of the Joint Committee shall be organized by a total of six members, three Japanese and three "Manchukuo" people (the Japanese side is the Chief of Staff of the Kwantung Army, the Director-General of the Kwantung Bureau, and the Counselor of the Embassy; the "Manchukuo" side is the Chief of the General Affairs Department, the Minister of Industry, and the Minister of Finance). Under the Committee, the two governments of Japan and "Manchukuo" shall appoint an equal number of executives.

'3. In order to handle the affairs of the Economic Joint Committee, a secretariat shall be established at the location of the Committee.

'4. The governments of Japan and "Manchukuo" shall submit to the Committee for deliberation all common economic matters related to both countries in the leased territory of Kwantung Prefecture ("Liaoli Peninsula region"). Other matters such as deliberation, suggestion, investigation, and reporting on the strategy of Japan-"Manchukuo" economic cooperation shall be handled by the Committee.

'5. The regulations on the powers of the Japan-"Manchukuo" Economic Joint Committee, whether the committee members, executives, and advisors are participated by knowledgeable people from the private sector, although it has not been decided at present, but the committee's powers, all regarding the economic development of "Manchukuo", the Kwantung Army Command has the guiding power. The powers of the above two, the policies adopted, and the functions of research, investigation, exchange of opinions, deliberation and consultation for adjusting the economic control of Japan and "Manchukuo", the committee is an organ with all these functions.'

From the above five organizational outlines, we can fully see the content of the so-called Japan-"Manchukuo" economic alliance. Moreover, it clearly pointed out in the fifth item that the Economic Joint Committee must be guided by the Kwantung Army, in other words, it is controlled by the Kwantung Army. Not only can the local people not participate, but also the capitalists in Japan cannot but obey the leadership of the military. Moreover, it is also preparing to further 'promote the economic relationship between "Manchukuo" and China', expand the power of the Kwantung Army, and form an economic alliance in the Far East. The operation of this kind of attempt in European and American countries is completely to use economic power to control, always taking financial capital and industrial and commercial capital as the center. The method used by Japan is very different, taking the military as the center, and using military force to solve everything. (Dalian, February 12)

He Yaozu Passes Through Hankou from Beijing to Hunan

Embassy Organization Expenses Determined and Will Depart Soon

Hankou Correspondence: He Yaozu, the newly appointed Ambassador to Turkey, arrived in Hankou on the 19th from Beijing by postal plane. On the 20th, he went to Hunan to visit relatives and will stay for a few days before returning to Hankou to wait for an audience with Chairman Chiang before going to Beijing to prepare to go abroad. The reporter interviewed Mr. He at the Yangtze River Hotel. According to him, since receiving the government's order to be the Ambassador to Turkey, he has been actively preparing everything, but he has not been able to travel for a long time because the embassy's expenses have not been determined. The embassy organization has been generally prepared, and it is planned to appoint Wang Fansheng as Counselor, He Fengshan, Li Wenxian, Wang Shifu, Ma Hongdao, etc. as Secretaries, Lu Feng as Attendant, and Li Yaoyu and Yao Zhuxiu as Secretaries. The expense budget has also been approved by the Executive Yuan and submitted to the Central Political Council for approval, generally equal to the embassy in Japan. He has already sent Counselor Wang Fansheng to Ankara, the capital of Turkey, via England to prepare for embassy affairs. He is scheduled to lead the rest of the staff on the Italian cruise ship Conto Rosso on the 13th of next month to take office. Turkey has become increasingly prosperous and strong after political reforms, and its international status has risen sharply. It has washed away the shame of being the sick man of the Near East and is closely related to our country's revitalization movement. After taking office, he will strive to promote Sino-Turkish relations in order to live up to the government's trust. As for the Sino-Turkish trade treaty, it is necessary to increase the commercial affairs of the two countries. He will first exchange opinions with the authorities of that country, and then follow the orders of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs to discuss and proceed. (19th)

Yu Yongnan, Former Director of Finance of Anhui, Murdered

Second Son and Two Grandsons Still Missing

Wuhu Correspondence: Yu Yongnan, the former Director of Finance of Anhui and once the Assistant Governor, was kidnapped by bandits in Guanzhuang Street, which belongs to Qianshan County, his hometown. His wife, second son, Zhu Xun, eldest grandson, Shi Mei, and grandson, Shi Shizhu, were also kidnapped. After the news of the case came, those in Wuhu who had a relationship with Mr. Yu planned to raise a large sum of money to find a way to rescue them. While they were running around, they suddenly received a telegram from Anqing from Mr. Yu's eldest son, Yun Xun, saying that his father (Yongnan) had been brutally murdered by bandits in Tuoling, at the junction of Qianshan, Taihu, and Wangjiang counties. It is rumored that his wife has been released, but his second son and two grandsons are still missing. As for the cause of the murder, it is said to be due to accumulated grievances with the bandits. Friends of Mr. Yu were all saddened by the news. After leaving the officialdom, Mr. Yu moved to the South Gate of Anqing. Because of the changes in the political situation in recent years, Mr. Yu was regarded as a senior in the political circles of this province, and generally several people came to ask for his introduction every day. In order to avoid the noise, Mr. Yu moved to Guanzhuang Street, his hometown in Qianshan, a year ago to retire and serve his mother. He assisted in local charitable undertakings in many ways. The year before last, he went to Shanghai to ask various charitable organizations for disaster relief in the county. He fell and injured his leg on the way. Although he recovered after medical treatment, he still felt inconvenience when walking and had to use a cane when going out. A few hours before he was kidnapped, the outside world was very tense. Mr. Yu initially suspected that it was a rural gambler who had lost a bet and was robbing, but he did not know that a large number of bandits had approached the village. After receiving several reports, he suddenly realized that he was heavily surrounded by bandits. Even if he wanted to escape, it was impossible. This was the general situation when he was kidnapped. Unexpectedly, he was killed in the shortest period of time, which is really tragic. (20th)

Jiangsu Farmers Bank Regulates Rural Finance

The Jiangsu Farmers Bank is the earliest farmers bank established among all provinces. Its purpose is to regulate rural finance and develop agricultural production. In recent years, it has progressed quite rapidly and has achieved considerable success in providing relief to rural areas. We have obtained information on the progress of its operations in the 23rd year from the bank itself, and record it as follows:

(1) Bank Capital: The bank's capital has increased annually. As of this year, in addition to the original capital of 2.2 million yuan, an additional capital of 1.4 million yuan has been added, totaling 3.6 million yuan.

(2) Branches and Offices: The branches and offices added in the 23rd year include Shanghai, Yixing, Jinshan, and Fengxian in Jiangnan; and Qingjiang, Suqian, Taixing, Baoying, Dongtai, Funing, Dongkan, and Lianshui in Jiangbei. Including the original branches and offices, there are a total of 22 branches, 14 offices, and 7 agency offices, totaling 43.

(3) Overall Bank Business: The total deposits and savings of the entire bank, as of recently, amount to more than 8.6 million yuan, an increase of approximately four times compared to the previous year. Loans are targeted at rural cooperatives, and are classified according to their nature, including seedling loans, storage pledge loans, and marketing loans. The coordinated implementation of these three types of loans is a characteristic of the bank's lending. The total amount of various loans for the entire year, excluding savings offices, is more than 7.595 million yuan, an increase of more than 4.96 million yuan compared to the previous year. Among the loan balances, "warehouse storage pledge" and "marketing loans" are the most numerous, accounting for nearly 60% of the total. The surplus for the 23rd year is 110,000 yuan.

(4) Business Situation: (A) Cooperative Business: The bank has worked hard to promote cooperative businesses and has achieved considerable results. Among the types of cooperative loans, seedling loans are the most common. In terms of the number of cooperatives, a total of 1,500 cooperatives received loans throughout the year, and in terms of the amount of loans, it totaled 2.4 million yuan. The amount of loans repaid on time by cooperatives accounted for more than 90%. (B) Agricultural Warehouses: Warehouse storage pledge is the most effective method for regulating agricultural product prices and is also the bank's central policy for regulating rural finance. Since last year, the bank has attached great importance to the management of warehouse storage pledge, and has established many agricultural warehouses in various places. According to statistics, warehouses have been established in 39 counties, with more than 170 warehouses. The total amount of storage pledge loans has reached more than 4 million yuan as of recently, of which 90% of those requesting pledge loans are small farmers. The storage quantity is as little as several sheng or one dou, and the pledge loan is no more than two or three jiao, which also shows the hardship of the rural economy. The stored items include rice, beans, wheat, miscellaneous grains, bean cakes, flour, silk, cotton, cloth, and sheepskins. It is estimated that each bank stores pledge loans of about 200,000 to 300,000 yuan, and some as much as 600,000 yuan. In addition, the bank's warehouses also handle processing and marketing. The more effective ones are the Dongting Warehouse in Wuxi, which has a larger scale and the latest rice milling machine, and the Anfeng Warehouse in Dongtai, which has the latest cotton ginning machine. There are also those that specialize in mortgaging agricultural tools, such as the Yugou Warehouse in Qingjiang, which pledges more than 30,000 agricultural tools. Although there are currently more than 170 agricultural warehouses handling storage pledge, given the abundance of agricultural products in Jiangsu Province, the need is still more than this. It is heard that the bank plans to expand to more than 250 warehouses and store pledge 6 million yuan in the 24th year. (C) Cooperative Marketing: The bank believes that agricultural products from various places cannot be transported and sold, making it difficult for rural finance to circulate flexibly. In order to handle the marketing of agricultural products for farmers' cooperatives in various places, a agricultural product marketing office has been established in Shanghai as a centralized marketing agency for agricultural products in the province, and branch offices have been established in Wuxi, Yancheng, Rugao, Xuzhou, Qingjiang, Taixian, and other inland areas to facilitate communication. The main tasks of the office are "cooperative marketing" and "cooperative purchasing." The former mainly involves rice, wheat, and wheat, followed by cotton, pigs, daylily, native cloth, soybeans, and flowers. The latter mainly involves fertilizers and seeds, followed by machinery, cotton yarn, cattle, and diesel. Since the office was established in May last year, it has been in operation for seven months until the end of the year, handling marketing and purchasing amounting to more than 1 million yuan. Regarding agency marketing, the method is that the branch offices in various places or the agricultural bank assist the cooperatives in collecting, processing, grading, and packaging agricultural products. At the same time, the bank advances funds and then handles shipping, insurance, and other procedures on their behalf. After the agricultural products arrive at their destination, all pier care, contact with warehouses, handling sales, and collecting payments are handled by the marketing office. The office also employs specialists to study and handle the marketing of miscellaneous grains, cotton, and pigs, in order to be meticulous. Farmers feel it is very convenient.

Songjiang

Bizarre Robbery Case

At the home of Zhu Qiutian, a farmer in the 20th Tu of the First District, at around 6:00 PM on the 14th day of this month (lunar calendar), five people suddenly arrived wearing various colors of clothing and carrying firearms. They fired shots to intimidate people and searched each room, smashing cabinets and boxes. While they were causing a commotion, nearby residents heard the noise and gathered a crowd. The five people, knowing that it would be difficult to escape, claimed to be winter defense militia from Xinqiao Town in the Third District. The crowd identified the five people as they were not wearing uniforms, had no symbols, and included He Guanchang, Zhang Zugen, and Qian Xiutang, all well-known ruffians. They immediately reported to the Xinqiao Public Security Lookout, who dispatched police to take the five people away. Now, villagers such as Yu Xuesheng are concerned about public safety and have petitioned the county government to investigate the matter thoroughly. It is heard that the county government has not received a report from the Public Security Bureau on this case, making it difficult to ascertain the truth, and the matter is quite bizarre. They have ordered the bureau to investigate the actual situation and bring the arrested criminals to justice for investigation.

Anti-Smoking Association Encourages Smokers to Confess

After the promulgation of the regulations on smokers confessing in this county, the County Anti-Smoking Committee, the County Party Department, the County Government, and the Public Security Education District Office and other agencies jointly organized propaganda teams to go to bustling places inside and outside the city to give speeches in rotation and promote the regulations as much as possible. They also distributed propaganda materials and pamphlets, and posted slogans everywhere. The district chiefs in each township district supervised the township Baojia chiefs to hold events at the same time, which was very lively. It is hoped that smokers who have not yet obtained licenses will confess within the time limit to avoid criminal charges. It is now known that Xia Fugeng, a private smoker from Zhalin and other places, went to the County Anti-Smoking Committee today to apply for confession. After filling out the confession application, the committee sent police to escort him to the smoking cessation center to be properly treated. They can be weaned off in about six or seven days. Secretary Yao of the committee gave Xia Fugeng and others encouragement and instructed the smoking cessation center to give them preferential treatment to assist and encourage them.

Dredging the City River and Building a Dam at Kaiyong

Dredging the city river in this county began last year, but was suspended due to disputes among the residents over the design and fundraising. However, the city river has become extremely shallow, and it is necessary to continue dredging for the people's drinking water and water transportation. County Magistrate Jin has ordered the First District Chief Li Zufu to be responsible for continuing the work. After convening local people to discuss solutions, the city river to be dredged was divided into six sections, and each section was assigned a director to preside over the project. The total cost, in addition to the allocation from the county construction fund, was short of about 8,000 yuan. District Chief Li also consulted with Chairman Cai of the Chamber of Commerce to raise funds. All sectors, recognizing the necessity of dredging the river, voluntarily donated enthusiastically. Bailongtan was not originally included in the dredging plan, but now, at the request of Cheng Weiru, a representative from the area, he volunteered to raise 800 yuan to dredge it. The Dredging Committee has appointed Vice Chairman Cai and Director Qian to conduct on-site surveys. The first section from Dongmenkou to Guangming Bridge Lane, as well as the third and sixth sections, began dredging yesterday with pile driving and dam construction, and are expected to be completed in about 20 days, followed by the other sections.

The Jiangsu Provincial Chamber of Commerce Federation Holds a Meeting in Wuxi

The Jiangsu Provincial Chamber of Commerce Federation held its February standing committee meeting of the executive committee in Wuxi yesterday (21st). On the same day, a joint meeting of executive and supervisory committee members was also held to discuss matters pending discussion by the federation. Chairman Yu Xiaochuan had previously obtained the consent of the Wuxi Chamber of Commerce and sent out notices inviting committee members from various places to come to Wuxi on time for the meeting. The committee members had arrived in Wuxi one after another in the afternoon of the previous day and stayed at the New World and Wuxi Hotels. At 9:00 AM yesterday, all the committee members took a steamship from the Dayou Stake Pier at Gongyun Bridge to Meiyuan, Xiaojishan, Yuantouzhu, and other places for sightseeing. At 12:00 noon, they had lunch at Chenglantang in Yuantouzhu. At about 2:00 PM, the meeting was held in Jingxiang Water Pavilion. The committee members present included Chairman Yu Xiaochuan (Zhenjiang), Standing Committee Wang Jingting (Jiangdu), Lan Bohua (Tongshan), Cheng Ganqing (Wuxian), Wu Suying (Wuxi), Zhu Zhongjing (Jiangyin), Pang Qinsheng (Yixing), Yin Jiquan (Wujiang), Gu Lunan (Zhenjiang), Dai Boqiu (Xinghua), Zhang Xiaoyou (Huaiyin), Supervisor Qian Chunyi (Taixing), and (Taicang). Those present included Yang Hanxi, Chairman of the Wuxi Chamber of Commerce, Cai Jiansan, Cheng Jingtang, Lin Junbao, Chairman of the Wujin Chamber of Commerce, and others. Chairman Yu Xiaochuan presided over the meeting and Li Bosen recorded the minutes. The matters discussed were as follows: (1) Chambers of Commerce in Jiading, Jiangyin, Wuxi, Yixing, Liyang, Minhang, Zhenjiang, Kunshan, Yancheng, and Taicang have repeatedly sent letters and telegrams stating that the Ministry of Finance has shortened the deadline for collecting business tax, which has a great impact on the future of commerce, and earnestly requested that the ministry be transferred to the provincial ministry to allow the cancellation of the order. How should the association handle this in order to achieve it? Resolved that the business tax is originally collected quarterly according to law. If it is regarded as overdue and a late fee is collected in the third month, it is contrary to the principles set by the central government. In the face of commercial decline, it is even more difficult to do so. The relevant departments of the central government should be immediately reported to inform Jiangsu Province to correct it. (2) The provincial government ordered the General Assembly of the China Aviation Association to send the articles of association for standardization and requested that the letters be transferred to the chambers of commerce in various places to invite local groups to form a branch within one month of the arrival of the letters. How should the association proceed in accordance with the order? Resolved that the letters should be divided into the chambers of commerce in various counties to carefully plan and proceed. (3) The Kunshan Chamber of Commerce applied to join the association as a member in accordance with the articles of association and requested that it be recognized so that a certificate could be issued. Resolved to pass. (4) The Wuxi Chamber of Commerce proposed to prevent speculation in cotton yarn and requested that it be transferred to the relevant ministries and councils of the central government to help cotton mills and maintain the livelihood of workers. Resolved to pass the proposal. The meeting adjourned at 3:30 PM. The committee members took the original ship to Baojie Changqiao for sightseeing, and then returned to the city. In the evening at 6:00 PM, the Wuxi Chamber of Commerce hosted a banquet for the committee members at the New World Western Restaurant to fulfill the obligations of the host. The members returned to their hometowns today.

Changzhou

Prosecution of the Caoqiao Murder Case

The Caoqiao Town murder case, which caused a sensation in the three counties of Wuxi, Yixing, and Yixing, initially identified Zhou Zhongsheng, the town chief and commander of the security corps of the town, as having an affair with the daughter of Renchun Sauce Garden. Later, the woman found another lover, causing Changsheng to become jealous and kill her, abandoning the body to eliminate traces, etc. Later, a body was found by Taihu Lake. After the prosecutors of Wujin and Yixing jointly examined it, it was the same as the case of abandoning the body in the murder case that was reported. Yang Kongyi, the chief prosecutor of the Wujin County Court, went to the countryside to investigate and repeatedly summoned the people involved in the case for interrogation, and the truth of the case began to emerge. Yesterday, the criminal court of the court was prosecuted. The content of the indictment recognized that Qiu Changsheng and Wei Baolin, members of the corps, killed an unknown person while on patrol. Zhou Fulian, the husband of a boatman, Han Chuanbao, abandoned the body. Zhou Zhongsheng, the head of the corps, could not prove that he had jealousy and murder, but as the head of the business corps, the corps members killed people and did not report it, and abetted the abandonment of the body and the destruction of evidence. The prosecution was based on legal provisions. The criminal court will summon witnesses to open a public trial within days.

Nantong

Execution of the Leader of the Jiangbei Sea Bandits

After the Jiangbei coastal sea bandits were suppressed by the various teams of the Third District of the Jiangsu Provincial Maritime Public Security Bureau, the bandit leader Zhuang Zhiwei was arrested at Taozikou and sent to the Fourth District Security Command of Nantong for interrogation. Commander Zheng sentenced the criminal to death for gathering crowds to rob the ocean and kidnapping people for ransom. The provincial government approved the sentence on the 20th and escorted him to the execution ground in the east of the city for execution.

Two Post Office Staff Members Abscond with Public Funds

Yi Peizhi, a staff member of the remittance office of the Nantong Post Office, and Tu Tingwan, a staff member of the ticket office, recently absconded with more than 2,000 yuan of public funds. Director Lan Songheng has reported to the Postal Administration for investigation.

Gaoyou

Investigation of the Private Sale of Opium

Family Members Bribing Arrested

The Jiangsu Provincial Anti-Smoking Committee recently sent investigators Wu Yeyong and others to Gaoyou to work. They first arrested Zhou Junqing and Wu Xiaoxian, who were privately selling opium, and sent them to the county government along with the private opium and account books they had seized. After questioning, they were first detained. Zhou Lisan and Wu Qi, family members, asked Jiang Xu, the female owner of the Zhonghua Lou Inn outside the North Gate, to bribe the investigator Wu, stating that it would be 200 yuan. Wu pretended to contact them. After the money was handed over, Wu immediately sent Zhou Lisan and Wu Qi, along with 150 yuan of the bribe money, to the county government for investigation. After the county government opened a court session, Zhou Lisan did not admit to bribery, but Wu Qi confessed. The court ordered Zhou Lisan to be detained (Zhou is also a private opium offender), and Wu Qi was released on bail from two merchants. The trial continued yesterday, and Jiang Xu, the female owner of the inn, was summoned to court. Zhou Lisan still did not admit to bribery, but Wu Qi accused Zhou Lisan of asking Jiang Xu to contact him. Zhou Lisan and Jiang Xu both swore that they did not admit it. Later, investigator Wu was summoned for questioning. Wu replied that Zhou and Wu had both come to see him, and Jiang Xu, the female owner of the inn, had also asked to be introduced, which was true. At this point, the court ordered Zhou Lisan to be detained, Wu Qi to be released on original bail, and Jiang Xu to be released on merchant bail, pending submission to the Provincial Anti-Smoking Association for review.

Xiaoshan

Tragic News of a Suicide by a Disaster Victim in the Western Countryside

Since the drought in the western countryside of Xiaoshan last year, the general poor people even lack food and clothing, and the sale of sons and daughters is heard every day. The most difficult are the disaster victims who are generally old, weak, and sick. There are several cases of death due to lack of food and clothing every day. Lai Chusheng, a farmer in Waisha, Puyang, was 70 years old. He died on the 15th due to freezing and starvation. In Yandou Sun, Sun Zuochen's mother died after five days of freezing and starvation. The grandmother of Zhou Ruisheng, a farmer in Shalangyu, committed suicide by hanging on the 16th because her three sons took turns supporting her, but each house lacked food and clothing.

Xiuning

The Third District Chief Was Killed in a Vendetta

Former Chief of the Third District of Xiuning County, Wang Hong, lived in Qianshan, the 52nd Bao of the First District. Unexpectedly, at about 11:00 PM on January 30th, a group of thugs suddenly came, speaking the local dialect and using boulders to break open the gate, surrounding the front and back. A part of them swarmed into the house, wielding iron rulers, wooden sticks, sharp knives, and other weapons, claiming that they must hand over Wang Hong. They searched everywhere upstairs and downstairs and finally found him. Without saying a word, they beat him with iron and wooden sticks, and he immediately fell to the ground unconscious. They stabbed him with sharp knives, his brains splashed everywhere, and his throat was pierced. He died on the spot, and the fierce people left. There was no loss of property in the house. His wife and eldest niece were also seriously injured at the same time. It was late at night, and the family, apart from Wang Hong himself, were all weak women and children and could not resist, resulting in this tragedy. Moreover, many of the thugs had cloth coverings on their faces, so it seemed like they were acquaintances. It is said that the victim's family has sued the county government, and it should not be difficult to find out the truth.

Local News

Ambassador Yan Departed for the Soviet Union Yesterday

Mei Lanfang and More Than Thirty Others Travel Together

Arrival in Moscow Expected on the Eighth or Ninth of Next Month

Dr. Yan Huiqing, China's ambassador to Russia, along with renowned opera singer Mei Lanfang and Zhou Jianyun and Hu Die, representatives of China's delegation to the Soviet Russian International Film Exhibition, and a party of more than thirty people, departed Shanghai yesterday aboard the Northern Steamer, taking a detour via Vladivostok to Russia. Details are recorded as follows:

Departure Yesterday

Ambassador Yan, Mr. Mei Lanfang, Mr. Zhou Jianyun, and Ms. Hu Die arrived at the China Merchants Bureau North Bund on Broadway Road one after another at around 1:00 PM yesterday. They boarded the Northern Steamer and mingled with the well-wishers in the passenger cabin. The steamer then set sail from Shanghai at around 3:00 PM in the afternoon, heading for Vladivostok. Ambassador Yan and others are scheduled to transfer to a special train upon arrival in Vladivostok and travel directly to Moscow.

Enthusiastic Farewell

Those who went to the pier yesterday to bid farewell to Ambassador Yan, Mei Lanfang, Zhou Jianyun, and Hu Die included Tang Shixuan, representative of Mayor Wu, Yang Hu, Chief of the Municipal Security Department, Xu Shiying of the National Government Disaster Relief Committee, Qian Xinzhi, General Manager of the Four Banks Savings Society, Liu Hongsheng, General Manager of the China Merchants Bureau, Du Yuesheng, Municipal Councilor, Spirvi, Soviet Russian Deputy Consul, Balkoff, Counselor, Mikolovski, and Gu Xin, Gao Zhanfei, and other male and female stars from the Star Company, totaling more than a hundred people. The Star Company also went to film newsreels, and the atmosphere at the pier was unusually enthusiastic.

Traveling Companions

Those who accompanied Ambassador Yan and Mei Lanfang on the same ship to Russia this time included playwright Yu Shangyuan, Zhang Pengchun, Professor of Nankai University, Zhou Jianyun and his wife, Hu Die, China's representatives to the Soviet Russian International Film Exhibition, Mrs. Wu Nanru, wife of the Chinese agent in Russia, Jiao Xiangzong and his wife, Secretary of the Embassy in Russia, Mrs. Wei, wife of Secretary Wei, Tian Baoqi and his wife, Vice-Consul in Vladivostok, Mrs. Xu Nianceng, wife of the Consul-General in Berlik, Yao Yuying, a dan (female) role in the Mei Lanfang Troupe, Wang Shaoting, an old male role, Yang Shengchun, a young male role, Liu Lianrong, a painted face role, Zhu Guifang, a female martial role, Wu Yuling, a male martial role, Xu Lanyuan, a musician and lute player, Huo Wenyuan, a string player, Ma Guiming, a flute player, Luo Wentian, a large gong player, Tang Xiguang, a small gong player, Liu Jianfang, a sheng (reed pipe wind instrument) player, He Binkui, a drummer, Sun Huiting, a moon lute player, and Han Peiting, who manages the props backstage. The total number of people, including attendants, is more than thirty. Mr. Mei was previously introduced by Feng Gengguang to purchase dozens of exquisite antique bronzes from the Meifeng Gold Foundry run by Jiang Xiaojian, which he brought to Russia this time to distribute to dignitaries in the diplomatic circles of Russia and Europe.

Mr. Yan's Speech

Ambassador Yan met with reporters from various newspapers on the ship yesterday and gave a speech before his departure. He said that at this time of serious national crisis, the people of the country must be sincere and united internally in order to achieve a consistent effect externally. At the same time, the people should have absolute faith in the government, and the government should be open and honest with the people. Only in this way can we work together to achieve a unified approach to the outside world.

Special Ship Direct Sailing

According to the crew member managing the Northern Steamer, the ship sailed directly from Shanghai to Vladivostok without passing through Kobe or Tsuruga in Japan because the ship was specially for transporting goods for the Association, so there was no need to stop in Japan. The journey from Shanghai to Vladivostok is expected to take six days. If there are no obstructions such as wind or fog along the way, it is expected to arrive in Vladivostok by the end of this month, and then transfer to another ship to Moscow, which will also take six or seven days, arriving in the Russian capital around the ninth of next month.

Mr. Mei's Speech

Mr. Mei Lanfang said in a conversation on the ship before his departure: (1) The Soviet Russian invitation was made last February and has been in contact for a year. I am very grateful for the government's encouragement and the support of all parties before the trip. (2) It was originally planned to go to France, England, and Italy to perform along the way, and to visit the theater arts of those countries in Central Europe for research purposes. Dr. Lalou, Secretary-General of the French National Theater, has repeatedly sent letters and telegrams stating that the director of the National Theater is very much looking forward to me performing in the theater and has prepared a very detailed plan, which is very touching. The British side was contacted by the British Foreign Office and Ambassador Guo Taiqi, who said that people in the theater industry in their country were very much looking forward to my performance for research purposes. The former Chinese ambassador to Italy sent an official letter stating that he had been ordered by the Roman government to invite me to perform in Italy. All of them could not be answered due to time constraints, which is very regrettable, because I will leave Russia at the earliest in late April, which is past the European theater season, and it is already summer, and the weather is getting hot, which is not suitable for theater performance. (3) A few days ago, I suddenly received a telegram from the Chinese Embassy in Russia saying that the Cultural Association requested to add two days of performances to the original scheduled performance date and to add one or two more plays because the theater industry in their country wanted to see more performances for research purposes. I have replied to the telegram agreeing to it. (4) After arriving in Russia this time, I plan to visit Sweden, Germany, France, England, Italy, Switzerland, Poland, and Greece after the performance, and to see the scenery. I will return to China around the end of summer and the beginning of autumn. In addition, the situation has been reported in the newspapers, so I will not repeat it. (5) When boarding the ship, I suddenly received a telegram from Ambassador Zhang Xinhai of Poland forwarded by Mr. Chu Minyi stating that the Polish authorities plan to invite me to perform for a few days when I pass through the Polish capital, according to the Soviet Union's hospitality principles, and I hope that I will agree. However, since England, France, and Italy have all contacted me, I have not been able to respond, so I am not able to agree alone. I plan to send a telegram of polite refusal after arriving in Russia. The Russian ship Northern is scheduled to arrive in Vladivostok on the 26th or 27th, and I should be able to arrive in Moscow by the 8th or 9th of next month at the latest. It is agreed to rest for seven or eight days before going on stage to perform, so that there will be no misunderstanding of the Soviet Russian government's schedule.

Hu Die on the Right, Mei Lanfang on the Left, and Zhang Ming on the Far Left

Mr. Zhou's Speech

According to Mr. Zhou Jianyun, the Soviet Russian International Film Exhibition opened yesterday. Economic Depression in Shanghai: Local Associations Discuss Relief Plans

Request Central Bank to Release Large Loans to Industry and Commerce

Both Chinese and Foreign Financial Institutions Increase Mortgage Lending on Real Estate

Shanghai is suffering from the overall economic downturn, resulting in an extraordinary decline. Local associations and other groups have repeatedly convened meetings to discuss recovery plans, requesting the Central Bank to release loans for relief, and Chinese and foreign financial circles are negotiating to undertake real estate mortgages. Details are as follows:

Local Associations Gather to Discuss Relief

The Shanghai Local Associations, jointly organized by leaders from various industries, recognizing the decline of various sectors, convened a joint meeting on February 3rd to discuss relief and recovery. They decided to form a subcommittee to study the matter. After several meetings, they met again yesterday afternoon and reportedly decided to proceed with both short-term and long-term solutions. For the short-term, they requested the Central Bank and other designated institutions to continue allocating funds for mortgage lending to provide some turnover in the market. For the long-term, due to the seriousness of the issue, they are still conducting further research.

Various Industries Request Loans for Support

A reporter from the New Voice News Agency learned from various important business sectors that they are facing extraordinary difficulties due to the economic downturn and the extraordinary decline in the market. Simultaneously, banks and financial institutions are being particularly cautious with lending to various industries, resulting in tight credit conditions. Furthermore, the Central Bank, Bank of China, and Bank of Communications are providing loans for support only to banks and financial institutions. Therefore, after discussions, they plan to jointly request the Central Bank to designate large sums of money for mortgage lending to various industries.

Financial Circles Discuss Real Estate Mortgages

The real estate industry has been affected by the economic downturn, leading to a sharp drop in prices. Various sectors now recognize that real estate represents the largest asset in Shanghai. Furthermore, real estate businessmen are typically engaged in other businesses as well, and the failure of a real estate businessman will inevitably affect other businesses, impacting the entire market. Chinese and foreign banks are deeply aware of this and have held discussions to provide support for real estate mortgages within the possible scope.

Foreign Exchange Market Prices Fall Consistently

The Foreign Exchange Equalization Committee announced yesterday at 10:00 AM that the equalization tax rate was 5.75%. The Central Bank's telegraphic transfer selling prices are as follows: London, one national currency unit equals one shilling and six pence; New York, one hundred national currency units equals thirty-six US dollars and sixty-two and a half cents; Paris, one hundred national currency units equals five hundred and fifty-two francs; Berlin, one hundred national currency units equals ninety and a half marks. These prices, which convert national currency to foreign currency, are slightly higher than those of the previous two days.

China Agricultural Loan Syndicate Invites Banks to Participate

Shaanxi Office Established and Loans Initiated

Offices in Henan, Hebei, Shandong, etc., to be Established by the End of the Month

The China Agricultural Loan Syndicate, organized by the Bank of Communications, Shanghai Commercial & Savings Bank, Kin Cheng Banking Corporation, Chekiang Industrial Bank, and the Farmers Bank of Four Provinces, established its office at the Bund branch of the Bank of Communications after its founding. Staff members were transferred from the Shanghai branches of the Bank of Communications to begin operations. A reporter from the New News Agency learned yesterday that the syndicate has decided to first establish offices in Henan, Hebei, Shandong, and Shaanxi provinces. The Shaanxi office has already been established in Xi'an, with Lu Zhigu appointed as director, and has begun lending. The other offices are to be fully established by the end of this month. Directors and staff members have been assigned. This year's plan is to provide three million in credit loans. Syndicate directors Zou Bingwen, Li Zhongchu, Zhu Runsheng, and Yang Yinpu plan to depart from Shanghai in mid-next month to inspect the offices after the offices in the four provinces have been established. Furthermore, in order to increase capital and expand the lending area, after the syndicate's charter is revised, printed, and ready, invitations will be sent to various banks to participate in the joint operation. It is reported that the Bank of China and the New China Trust & Savings Bank are prepared to participate, as these two banks have consistently supported agricultural lending and have already implemented it.

Financial Advisory Committee to Hold Subcommittee Meetings

To Study Issues such as Stabilizing Exchange Rates

The New News Agency reports that the Financial Advisory Committee, organized by the Ministry of Finance, was formally established on the 16th of this month. The appointed members are all experienced financiers. The committee's mission is to plan methods for stabilizing finance and recommend them to the government for implementation. Recently, there have been widespread rumors that the committee's first step towards stabilizing finance is to prepare for international exchange control. A reporter from the New News Agency visited various members of the committee yesterday morning to inquire about the truth. All members stated that they were unwilling to express any opinions before the government made a decision on the matter. However, according to another source, Minister of Finance Kung believes that various financial issues, such as stabilizing exchange rates and adjusting domestic finance, need to be studied. The Financial Advisory Committee will convene a subcommittee meeting in the coming days to jointly study them, and then submit the research results to the government for reference and implementation.

Borrowers of Loans from the Central Bank and Other Banks Request Renewal

Over Five Million Still Outstanding

The Central Bank, Bank of China, and Bank of Communications jointly released over seven million in mortgage loans at the end of the last major period to stabilize the financial market. A reporter from the New News Agency learned from the Central Bank yesterday that over five million of these loans remain outstanding as of yesterday, and the borrowers are requesting renewal. However, the Central Bank and the other two banks require only that borrowers pay interest on time. Therefore, the principal of the loans will not be urged for repayment. In the future, if new borrowers request loans, they will be considered based on the situation. These loans are entirely for the purpose of adjusting financial circulation in the market.

Five Banks Act as Agents for Collecting Aviation Donations

Headquarters of the General Team Determines Measures

Since the China Aviation Association's Headquarters of the Solicitation Team began its second fundraising campaign, various activities have been carried out with great effort. In order to facilitate communication with the team leaders, the general team leader has appointed Secretary-General Li Dachao and Secretaries Zhang Yuliang, Xue Baolun, Zhou Songhe, Zhu Shengyang, Zhou Xin, Li Jiming, and Gu Shangrui to contact the team leaders at any time and assist in the fundraising. The headquarters has now finalized the previous plan, and the staff members familiar with the situation have been assigned to contact several team leaders and assist with all matters related to the fundraising. It is reported that activities will begin separately today.

Furthermore, the Headquarters of the Solicitation Team has decided to request the Central Bank, Bank of China, Bank of Communications, Shanghai Commercial & Savings Bank, and Shanghai Municipal Bank to act as agents for collecting membership fees and donations submitted by the team leaders. In order to unify and facilitate the process, the headquarters has established five measures for the agency collection, as follows: (1) The Headquarters of the Shanghai Solicitation Team of the China Aviation Association has specially entrusted the Central Bank, Bank of China, Bank of Communications, Shanghai Commercial & Savings Bank, and Shanghai Municipal Bank to act as agents for collecting membership fees and donations submitted by the team leaders of various solicitation teams in order to unify and facilitate the process. (2) The banks will act as agents for collecting membership fees and donations from the team leaders for a period of six months, which may be extended if necessary. (3) When the banks receive membership fees and donations from the team leaders, the first copy of the membership fee receipt and donation receipt issued by the headquarters will be given to the payer for safekeeping, and the second copy will be submitted to the headquarters. At the end of the period, the third copy of the stub and any unused receipts will be sent to the headquarters for verification. (4) The banks should notify the headquarters of the amount of membership fees and donations collected by the team leaders at any time for publication. (5) If the team leaders need more receipts, they can obtain them from the headquarters on the third floor of the YMCA at the Eight Immortals Bridge.

Banks to Increase Investment in Rural Areas This Spring

Accounting for One-Fifth of Savings

According to sources in Shanghai's banking community, in recent years, banks in Shanghai have concentrated cash in cities, while the market has been depressed and all industries have declined. Although the banks have profits, they are abnormal. Therefore, in order to seek the development of banking operations, it is necessary to seek the development of various industries. Adjusting rural finance is the foundation for the development of all industries. Bankers with vision advocate investing in the interior and adjusting the rural economy. Banks such as the Bank of China and the Shanghai Commercial & Savings Bank first invested in rural areas and have achieved considerable results. Therefore, banks followed suit, and the rural areas have achieved significant results through the investment adjustment of various banks last year. At the same time, many banks have also profited from investing in rural areas. Therefore, the authorities of various banks have decided to increase investment in rural areas this spring. The amount of investment will account for one-fifth of the savings of various banks. The rural areas had a bumper harvest last year, and after this adjustment, the rural areas will inevitably develop day by day, and the relationship with social finance is not superficial.

Ancient Artifacts for London Exhibition to be Displayed in Mid-March

Exhibition Period Set for Three Weeks, Venue Being Prepared

The London International Exhibition of Chinese Art has leased Burlington House in London as its venue and is scheduled to officially open in November this year. This exhibition will introduce all ancient artifacts and art from Chinese dynasties to the international community, which is very important. Therefore, the search for exhibits is very comprehensive, from ancient times to 1800. The Chinese government has agreed to transport a portion of the ancient artifacts from the ancient artifact exhibition hall in Shanghai, which are rare treasures, for display. In order to ensure dedicated handling, the Preparatory Committee for the London International Exhibition of Chinese Art was established in Nanjing, with Minister of Education Wang Shijie specially responsible for all matters. The ancient artifacts were originally planned to be publicly exhibited once after arriving in Shanghai, but it was not realized due to the large number of boxes, complicated procedures, and lack of suitable locations. Now that the ancient artifacts will be selected and transported to London for exhibition, this opportunity is taken to first publicly exhibit them in Shanghai to allow people to appreciate Chinese artifacts and understand the exact number of artifacts being transported to England. The Bank of China on the Bund is renovating its old building and moving its office to the Third Road. The committee contacted the bank authorities to lease the old site as its Shanghai office and prepare to exhibit some ancient artifacts on the second and third floors for several days. Yesterday, a reporter from the Central News Agency visited Tang Xifen, secretary of the Shanghai Preparatory Office, to inquire about the latest situation of the exhibition. Tang's remarks are recorded as follows:

Preparing the Venue

According to Tang, the office has moved into the new site for many days and is actively repairing the office buildings. The exhibition venue is being designed by architect Li Jinpei, who is voluntarily designing and arranging the venue (he is also planning and designing the warehouse in the capital that will store the ancient artifacts of the Palace Museum, costing 600,000 yuan). More than 10,000 yuan has been used to order 64 steel-framed glass cabinets from the Dahua Iron Factory for displaying art objects in the exhibition. For the safety of the ancient artifacts, iron fences are being installed at the exits of the venue and warehouse. The original electric lights and wires of the Bank of China have been reinstalled to avoid fire. The Public Concession Police Department has also agreed to provide special police protection.

Discussion and Review

The committee held its fifth specialized committee meeting at the Shanghai Preparatory Office on the afternoon of the 19th to discuss and review the exhibition items. Attendees included Xu Beihong, Deng Shucun, Ma Heng, Xu Hongbin (represented by Ouyang Daoda), Li Ji, Tang Lan, Yang Zhensheng, Guo Baochang, and Rong Geng (represented by Tang Lan). Gu Shusen attended as an observer. Three resolutions were decided: (1) Review the preliminary selection catalog, divided into three categories: calligraphy and painting, porcelain, and bronze. (2) Review will be conducted on Catholic Church Street this week and at the committee's warehouse next week. (3) Review will be conducted in groups: the calligraphy and painting group will be responsible for reviewing by Xu Beihong, Yang Zhensheng, Deng Shucun, Gu Shusen, and Ye Gongchuo; the porcelain group will be responsible for reviewing by Guo Baochang and Zhang Changyun; and the bronze group will be responsible for reviewing by Tang Lan, Li Ji, Xu Hongbin, and Ma Heng.

Planning the Exhibition

The exhibition will open in mid-March and close three weeks later. The catalog of ancient artifacts is currently being translated into English by Zhang Changyun, consultant to the committee, to facilitate appreciation by foreigners during the exhibition. The price of admission tickets has not yet been determined, but the preparations require funding, so it will not be less than two yuan. In the past, visitors to Beijing who wanted to visit the ancient artifacts of the Palace Museum had to take three routes, each with a daily ticket price of one yuan. Now that ancient artifacts from various places are gathered in one place, the ticket price will be higher, but the audience will not be affected. However, for the safety of the ancient artifacts and the order of the venue, the daily number of visitors has been limited to 2,000.

Shanghai West Power and Water Taken Back for Self-Management

Municipal Government Borrowed 1.5 Million

Approved by the Executive Yuan Review Committee

The Central News Agency reported from Nanjing on the 21st that the Executive Yuan's Review Committee held a meeting at 9:00 AM on the 21st, attended by Chu Minyi, Peng Xuepei, representatives from the Ministry of Finance and the Ministry of Industry, and Cai Zengji, Director of the Shanghai Finance Bureau. The meeting was to review the Shanghai Municipal Government's plan to borrow 1.5 million to take over the Shanghai West Power and Water business. In order to take back the Shanghai West power rights, it is necessary to build a power and water plant for self-management. After drafting a plan, it was proposed to borrow money to start the business and submit it to the Executive Yuan for record. It is reported that the Executive Yuan has approved the review.

National Products Promotion Conference to Open in Mid-March

Application Submitted to Party and Government Agencies Yesterday for Record

Lin Kanghou Wrote to Kuang Zhongmou to Discuss Borrowing the Venue

The Shanghai National Products Promotion Conference, initiated by the China National Products Manufacturers Association, was postponed due to the approaching end of the traditional New Year. The association extended the deadline at the request of various factories. It is reported that the association has been receiving letters from disaster relief groups in various provinces, counties, and cities. The originally borrowed venue on the opposite side of the Great World is now unavailable because the landowner, Zhang Danru, has left Shanghai. Therefore, Lin Kanghou, chairman of the National Federation of Commerce, wrote to Kuang Zhongmou to discuss borrowing the vacant land of the Penglai Market as the conference venue and scheduled the official opening for March 15th. Details are as follows:

Application for Record

The China National Products Manufacturers Association submitted a document to the Municipal Party Department and the Social Affairs Bureau yesterday for record of holding the Shanghai National Products Promotion Conference. The document stated: "In recent years, water and drought have caused disasters, and Heaven has afflicted China. At this time of national crisis, rural collapse, and extreme social and economic panic, unfortunately, Zhejiang and Jiangsu provinces have suffered severe droughts again last year. The disaster is especially severe in eastern Zhejiang, with thousands of miles of red land, almost no harvest, and hungry and cold cries shaking the fields. The tragic situation is unprecedented. Mencius said, 'The heart of compassion is possessed by all men.' How can we not be saddened by the disaster victims who are waiting to be fed? Zhejiang and Jiangsu provinces have always been known for their abundant products, and the prosperity of Shanghai's national product industry is also linked to this. Now that Zhejiang Province has suffered this unprecedented catastrophe, how can we turn a blind eye and not seek relief? In view of this, our association, based on the principle of gathering little to make much and accumulating sand to build a tower, has specially organized the Shanghai National Products Promotion Conference. The vacant land of the Penglai Market at Xiaoximen has been identified as the venue, and the official opening is scheduled for March 15th. The conference will last for three weeks. In addition to displaying national product exhibitions and establishing a temporary national product market, a recreation area will be opened near the conference to stage patriotic dramas or show national product films to entertain guests. Admission tickets will be distributed by various manufacturers with their goods, and the income from the tickets will be donated to disaster relief to help the victims. The method is good and the intention is beautiful, which is a win-win situation. In addition to applying to the Municipal Party Department (Social Affairs Bureau) for record, we respectfully submit this document to your council (bureau) for review. We respectfully request your approval for the record for the public convenience."

Lin's Letter to Kuang

The conference venue was originally discussed by Chu Huiseng, chairman of the Jiaxu Association, with Zhang Danru, using the vacant land opposite the Great World as the venue. However, Zhang has gone to another place, so there is no way to contact him. Therefore, Liu Zhongying, a member of the Standing Committee of the China National Products Manufacturers Association, wrote to Kuang Zhongmou, the owner of the Penglai Market, proposing to borrow the market as the venue. Kuang expressed his deep approval of the association's purpose of promoting national products and helping disaster victims. However, the vacant land had already been introduced by Lin Kanghou, chairman of the National Federation of Commerce, to the National Products Business Publishing House for a national products exhibition and had not yet been finalized.
